</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">[</span><span class="n">rum</span> <span class="nl">stopViewWithViewController</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">self</span> <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">nil</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>For more details and available options, see <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios/blob/master/DatadogRUM/Sources/RUMMonitorProtocol.swift"><code>RUMMonitorProtocol</code> in GitHub</a>.</p><h3 id="custom-actions-2">Custom actions</h3><p>In addition to <a href="#automatically-track-user-actions">tracking actions automatically</a>, you can track specific custom user actions (taps, clicks, and scrolls) with the <code>addAction(type:name:)</code> API.</p><p>To manually register instantaneous RUM actions such as <code>.tap</code> on <code>RUMMonitor.shared()</code>, use <code>.addAction(type:name:)</code>. For continuous RUM actions such as <code>.scroll</code>, use <code>.startAction(type:name:)</code> or <code>.stopAction(type:)</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogRUM</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in your `UIViewController`:</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">rum</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">RUMMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">@IBAction</span> <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">didTapDownloadResourceButton</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kc">_</span> <span class="n">sender</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIButton</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addAction</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">type</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">tap</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">sender</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">currentTitle</span> <span class="p">??</span> <span class="s">&#34;&#34;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">-</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">IBAction</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="nf">didTapDownloadResourceButton:</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">UIButton</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="nv">sender</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">NSString</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="n">name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">sender</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">currentTitle</span> <span class="o">?</span> <span class="n">sender</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nl">currentTitle</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">@&#34;&#34;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMMonitor</span> <span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">addActionWithType</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">DDRUMActionTypeTap</span> <span class="nl">name</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">name</span> <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p><strong>Note</strong>: When using <code>.startAction(type:name:)</code> and <code>.stopAction(type:)</code>, the action <code>type</code> must be the same. This is necessary for the RUM iOS SDK to match an action start with its completion.</p><p>For more details and available options, see <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios/blob/master/DatadogRUM/Sources/RUMMonitorProtocol.swift"><code>RUMMonitorProtocol</code> in GitHub</a>.</p><h3 id="custom-resources-2">Custom resources</h3><p>In addition to <a href="#automatically-track-network-requests">tracking resources automatically</a>, you can also track specific custom resources such as network requests or third-party provider APIs. Use the following methods on <code>RUMMonitor.shared()</code> to manually collect RUM resources:</p><ul><li><code>.startResource(resourceKey:request:)</code></li><li><code>.stopResource(resourceKey:response:)</code></li><li><code>.stopResourceWithError(resourceKey:error:)</code></li><li><code>.stopResourceWithError(resourceKey:message:)</code></li></ul><p>For example:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogRUM</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in your network client:</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">rum</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">RUMMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">startResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">resourceKey</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">request</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">stopResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">resourceKey</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">response</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">response</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in your network client:
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMMonitor</span> <span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">startResourceWithResourceKey</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;resource-key&#34;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                            <span class="nl">request</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">request</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                         <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMMonitor</span> <span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">stopResourceWithResourceKey</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;resource-key&#34;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                          <span class="nl">response</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">response</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                        <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p><strong>Note</strong>: The <code>String</code> used for <code>resourceKey</code> in both calls must be unique for the resource you are calling. This is necessary for the RUM iOS SDK to match a resource's start with its completion.</p><p>For more details and available options, see <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios/blob/master/DatadogRUM/Sources/RUMMonitorProtocol.swift"><code>RUMMonitorProtocol</code> in GitHub</a>.</p><h3 id="custom-errors-2">Custom errors</h3><p>To track specific errors, notify <code>RUMMonitor.shared()</code> when an error occurs using one of following methods:</p><ul><li><code>.addError(message:)</code></li><li><code>.addError(error:)</code></li></ul><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">rum</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">RUMMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">message</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;error message.&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMMonitor</span> <span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">addErrorWithMessage</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;error message.&#34;</span> <span class="nl">stack</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">nil</span> <span class="nl">source</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">DDRUMErrorSourceCustom</span> <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>For more details and available options, see <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios/blob/master/DatadogRUM/Sources/RUMMonitorProtocol.swift"><code>RUMMonitorProtocol</code> in GitHub</a> and the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/ios/data_collected/?tab=error#error-attributes">Error Attributes documentation</a>.</p><h2 id="track-custom-global-attributes-2">Track custom global attributes</h2><p>In addition to the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/ios/data_collected/?tab=session#default-attributes">default RUM attributes</a> captured by the RUM iOS SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information (such as custom attributes) to your RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog.</p><p>Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (such as the cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, and network health).</p><div class="alert alert-info"><p>Custom attributes are intended for small, targeted pieces of information (for example, IDs, flags, or short labels). Avoid attaching large objects such as full HTTP response payloads. This can significantly increase event size and impact performance.</p></div><h3 id="set-a-custom-global-attribute">Set a custom global attribute</h3><p>To set a custom global attribute, use <code>RUMMonitor.shared().addAttribute(forKey:value:)</code>.</p><ul><li>To add an attribute, use <code>RUMMonitor.shared().addAttribute(forKey: &quot;&lt;KEY&gt;&quot;, value: &quot;&lt;VALUE&gt;&quot;)</code>.</li><li>To update the value, use <code>RUMMonitor.shared().addAttribute(forKey: &quot;&lt;KEY&gt;&quot;, value: &quot;&lt;UPDATED_VALUE&gt;&quot;)</code>.</li><li>To remove the key, use <code>RUMMonitor.shared().removeAttribute(forKey: &quot;&lt;KEY_TO_REMOVE&gt;&quot;)</code>.</li></ul><p>For better performance in bulk operations (modifying multiple attributes at once), use <code>.addAttributes(_:)</code> and <code>.removeAttributes(forKeys:)</code>.</p><p><strong>Note</strong>: You can't create facets on custom attributes if you use spaces or special characters in your key names. For example, use <code>forKey: &quot;store_id&quot;</code> instead of <code>forKey: &quot;Store ID&quot;</code>.</p><h3 id="track-user-sessions-2">Track user sessions</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions makes it possible to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users</li></ul><a href="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?fit=max&amp;auto=format" class="pop" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#popupImageModal"><div class="shortcode-wrapper shortcode-img expand"><figure class="text-center"><picture><img srcSet="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?auto=format" class="img-fluid" alt="User API in the RUM UI"/></picture></figure></div></a><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use the <code>Datadog.setUserInfo(id:name:email:)</code> API.</p><p>For example:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogCore</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setUserInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">id</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;1234&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;John Doe&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">email</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;john@doe.com&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">DDDatadog</span> <span class="nl">setUserInfoWithId</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;1234&#34;</span> <span class="nl">name</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;John Doe&#34;</span> <span class="nl">email</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;john@doe.com&#34;</span> <span class="nl">extraInfo</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><h2 id="track-background-events">Track background events</h2><div class="alert alert-info"><p>Tracking background events may lead to additional sessions, which can impact billing. For questions, <a href="https://docs.datadoghq.com/help/">contact Datadog support</a>.</p></div><p>You can track events such as crashes and network requests when your application is in the background (for example, no active view is available).</p><p>To track background events, add the following snippet during initialization in your Datadog configuration:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogRUM</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">enable</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">with</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Configuration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">...</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">trackBackgroundEvents</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="initialization-parameters-2">Initialization parameters</h2><p>You can use the following properties in <code>Datadog.Configuration</code> when creating the Datadog configuration to initialize the library:</p><dl><dt><code>backgroundTasksEnabled</code></dt><dd>This flag determines if the <code>UIApplication</code> methods <code>beginBackgroundTask(expirationHandler:)</code> and <code>endBackgroundTask:</code> are used to perform background uploads. Enabling this flag might increase the amount of time that the app operates in the background by 30 seconds. Tasks are normally stopped when there's nothing to upload or when encountering a blocker to uploading, such as having no internet connection or having a low battery. By default, this flag is set to <code>false</code>.</dd><dt><code>batchProcessingLevel</code></dt><dd>Batch processing level defines the maximum number of batches processed sequentially without a delay within one reading/uploading cycle. The default value is <code>.medium</code>.</dd><dt><code>batchSize</code></dt><dd>Sets the preferred size of batched data uploaded to Datadog. This value impacts the size and number of requests performed by the RUM iOS SDK (small batches mean more requests, but each request becomes smaller in size). Available values include: <code>.small</code>, <code>.medium</code>, and <code>.large</code>.</dd><dt><code>bundle</code></dt><dd>The bundle object that contains the current executable.</dd><dt><code>clientToken</code></dt><dd>Either the RUM client token (which supports RUM, Logging, and APM) or the regular client token (which supports Logging and APM).</dd><dt><code>encryption</code></dt><dd>Data encryption to use for on-disk data persistency by providing an object that complies with the <code>DataEncryption</code> protocol.</dd><dt><code>env</code></dt><dd>The environment name that is sent to Datadog. This can be used to filter events by different environments (such as <code>staging</code> or <code>production</code>).</dd><dt><code>proxyConfiguration</code></dt><dd>A proxy configuration attribute which can be used to enable a custom proxy for uploading tracked data to Datadog's intake.</dd><dt><code>serverDateProvider</code></dt><dd>A custom NTP synchronization interface. By default, the Datadog SDK synchronizes with dedicated NTP pools provided by the <a href="https://www.ntppool.org/en/">NTP Pool Project</a>. Using different pools or setting a no operation <code>ServerDateProvider</code> implementation results in a de-synchronization of the SDK instance and the Datadog servers. This can lead to significant time shifts in RUM sessions or distributed traces.</dd><dt><code>service</code></dt><dd>The service name associated with data sent to Datadog. The default value is the application bundle identifier.</dd><dt><code>site</code></dt><dd>The Datadog server endpoint that data is sent to. The default value is <code>.us1</code>.</dd><dt><code>uploadFrequency</code></dt><dd>The preferred frequency of uploading data to Datadog. Available values include: <code>.frequent</code>, <code>.average</code>, and <code>.rare</code>.</dd></dl><h3 id="rum-configuration">RUM configuration</h3><p>You can use the following properties in <code>RUM.Configuration</code> when enabling RUM:</p><dl><dt><code>actionEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the data scrubbing callback for actions. This can be used to modify or drop action events before they are sent to Datadog. For more information, see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>.</dd><dt><code>appHangThreshold</code></dt><dd>Sets the threshold for reporting when an app hangs. The minimum allowed value for this option is <code>0.1</code> seconds. To disable reporting, set this value to <code>nil</code>. For more information, see <a href="/real_user_monitoring/error_tracking/mobile/ios/#add-app-hang-reporting">Add app hang reporting</a>.</dd><dt><code>applicationID</code></dt><dd>The RUM application identifier.</dd><dt><code>customEndpoint</code></dt><dd>A custom server URL for sending RUM data.</dd><dt><code>errorEventMapper</code></dt><dd>The data scrubbing callback for errors. This can be used to modify or drop error events before they are sent to Datadog. For more information, see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>.</dd><dt><code>longTaskEventMapper</code></dt><dd>The data scrubbing callback for long tasks. This can be used to modify or drop long task events before they are sent to Datadog. For more information, see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>.</dd><dt><code>longTaskThreshold</code></dt><dd>The threshold for RUM long tasks tracking (in seconds). By default, this is set to <code>0.1</code> seconds.</dd><dt><code>networkSettledResourcePredicate</code></dt><dd>The predicate used to classify &quot;initial&quot; resources for the Time-to-Network-Settled (TNS) view timing calculation.</dd><dt><code>nextViewActionPredicate</code></dt><dd>The predicate used to classify the &quot;last&quot; action for the Interaction-to-Next-View (INV) timing calculation.</dd><dt><code>onSessionStart</code></dt><dd>(Optional) The method that gets called when RUM starts the session.</dd><dt><code>resourceEventMapper</code></dt><dd>The data scrubbing callback for resources. This can be used to modify or drop resource events before they are sent to Datadog. For more information, see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>.</dd><dt><code>sessionSampleRate</code></dt><dd>The sampling rate for RUM sessions. The <code>sessionSampleRate</code> value must be between <code>0.0</code> and <code>100.0</code>. A value of <code>0.0</code> means no sessions are sent, while <code>100.0</code> means that all sessions are sent to Datadog. The default value is <code>100.0</code>.</dd><dt><code>telemetrySampleRate</code></dt><dd>The sampling rate for the SDK internal telemetry utilized by Datadog. This rate controls the number of requests reported to the tracing system. This must be a value between <code>0</code> and <code>100</code>. By default, this is set to <code>20</code>.</dd><dt><code>trackAnonymousUser</code></dt><dd>When enabled, the SDK generates a unique, non-personal anonymous user ID that is persisted across app launches. This ID is attached to each RUM Session, allowing you to link sessions originating from the same user/device without collecting personal data. By default, this is set to <code>true</code>.</dd><dt><code>trackBackgroundEvents</code></dt><dd>Determines whether RUM events are tracked when no view is active. By default, this is set to <code>false</code>.</dd><dt><code>trackFrustrations</code></dt><dd>Determines whether automatic tracking of user frustrations is enabled. By default, this is set to <code>true</code>.</dd><dt><code>trackMemoryWarnings</code></dt><dd>Determines whether automatic tracking of memory warnings is enabled. By default, this is set to <code>true</code>.</dd><dt><code>trackWatchdogTerminations</code></dt><dd>Determines whether the SDK should track application terminations performed by Watchdog. The default setting is <code>false</code>.</dd><dt><code>uiKitActionsPredicate</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking user interactions (taps) as RUM actions. You can use the default implementation of <code>predicate</code> by setting the <code>DefaultUIKitRUMActionsPredicate</code> or implement <a href="#automatically-track-user-actions">your own <code>UIKitRUMActionsPredicate</code></a> customized for your app.</dd><dt><code>uiKitViewsPredicate</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking <code>UIViewControllers</code> as RUM views. You can use default implementation of <code>predicate</code> by setting the <code>DefaultUIKitRUMViewsPredicate</code> or implement <a href="#automatically-track-views">your own <code>UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</code></a> customized for your app.</dd><dt><code>urlSessionTracking</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking <code>URLSession</code> tasks (network requests) as RUM resources. The <code>firstPartyHostsTracing</code> parameter defines hosts that are categorized as <code>first-party</code> resources (if RUM is enabled) and have tracing information injected (if tracing feature is enabled). The <code>resourceAttributesProvider</code> parameter defines a closure to provide custom attributes for intercepted resources that is called for each resource collected by the RUM iOS SDK. This closure is called with task information and may return custom resource attributes or <code>nil</code> if no attributes should be attached.</dd><dt><code>viewEventMapper</code></dt><dd>The data scrubbing callback for views. This can be used to modify view events before they are sent to Datadog. For more information, see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>.</dd><dt><code>vitalsUpdateFrequency</code></dt><dd>The preferred frequency for collecting mobile vitals. Available values include: <code>.frequent</code> (every 100ms), <code>.average</code> (every 500ms), <code>.rare</code> (every 1s), and <code>.never</code> (which disables vitals monitoring).</dd></dl><h3 id="automatically-track-views-2">Automatically track views</h3><p>You can automatically track views with UIKit and SwiftUI.</p><h4 id="uikit">UIKit</h4><p>To automatically track views (<code>UIViewControllers</code>), use the <code>uiKitViewsPredicate</code> option when enabling RUM. By default, views are named with the view controller's class name. To customize it, provide your own implementation of the <code>predicate</code> which conforms to <code>UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</code> protocol:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kd">protocol</span> <span class="nc">UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">viewController</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIViewController</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">?</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">@objc</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kd">protocol</span> <span class="nc">DDUIKitRUMViewsPredicate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">AnyObject</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">viewController</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIViewController</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">DDRUMView</span><span class="p">?</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>Inside the <code>rumView(for:)</code> implementation, your app should decide if a given <code>UIViewController</code> instance should start a RUM view (return a value) or not (return <code>nil</code>). The returned <code>RUMView</code> value must specify the <code>name</code> and may provide additional <code>attributes</code> for the created RUM view.</p><p>For instance, you can configure the predicate to use explicit type check for each view controller in your app:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">YourCustomPredicate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">viewController</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIViewController</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">?</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">switch</span> <span class="n">viewController</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">case</span> <span class="k">is</span> <span class="n">HomeViewController</span><span class="p">:</span>     <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="kd">init</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;Home&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">case</span> <span class="k">is</span> <span class="n">DetailsViewController</span><span class="p">:</span>  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="kd">init</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;Details&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">default</span><span class="p">:</span>                        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="kc">nil</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@interface</span> <span class="nc">YourCustomPredicate</span> : <span class="nc">NSObject</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">DDUIKitRUMViewsPredicate</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">([</span><span class="n">viewController</span> <span class="nl">isKindOfClass</span><span class="p">:[</span><span class="n">DetailsViewController</span> <span class="k">class</span><span class="p">]])</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMView</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">initWithName</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;Details&#34;</span> <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nb">nil</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>You can even come up with a more dynamic solution depending on your app's architecture.</p><p>For example, if your view controllers use <code>accessibilityLabel</code> consistently, you can name views by the value of accessibility label:</p><div class='code-tabs'>

      </div><p><strong>Note</strong>: The RUM iOS SDK calls <code>rumView(for:)</code> many times while your app is running. Datadog recommends keeping its implementation fast and single-threaded.</p><h4 id="swiftui">SwiftUI</h4><p>To automatically track views with SwiftUI, use the <code>swiftUIViewsPredicate</code> option when enabling RUM.</p><p>The mechanism to extract a SwiftUI view name relies on reflection. As a result, view names may not always be meaningful. If a meaningful name cannot be extracted, a generic name such as <code>AutoTracked_HostingController_Fallback</code> or <code>AutoTracked_NavigationStackController_Fallback</code> is used.</p><p>You can use the default predicate (<code>DefaultSwiftUIRUMViewsPredicate</code>) or provide your own implementation of the <code>SwiftUIRUMViewsPredicate</code> protocol to customize or filter view names.</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kd">protocol</span> <span class="nc">SwiftUIRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">extractedViewName</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">String</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">?</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Example: Custom predicate to ignore fallback names and rename views</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">CustomSwiftUIPredicate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">SwiftUIRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">extractedViewName</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">String</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">?</span> <span class="p">{</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;Special&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">extractedViewName</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@protocol</span> <span class="nc">DDSwiftUIRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">NSObject</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p><strong>Notes:</strong></p><ul><li>Datadog recommends enabling UIKit view tracking as well, even if your app is built entirely with SwiftUI.</li><li>Tab bars are not tracked automatically. Use <a href="#custom-views">manual tracking</a> for each tab view to track them.</li><li>If you use both automatic and manual tracking, you may see duplicate events. To avoid this, rely on a single instrumentation method or use a custom predicate to filter out duplicates.</li></ul><h3 id="automatically-track-user-actions">Automatically track user actions</h3><h4 id="uikit-2">UIKit</h4><p>To automatically track user tap actions with UIKit, set the <code>uiKitActionsPredicate</code> option when enabling RUM.</p><h4 id="swiftui-2">SwiftUI</h4><p>To automatically track user tap actions in SwiftUI, enable the <code>swiftUIActionsPredicate</code> option when enabling RUM.</p><p><strong>Notes:</strong></p><ul><li>Datadog recommends enabling UIKit action tracking as well even for pure SwiftUI apps as many interactive components rely on UIKit internally.</li><li>On tvOS, only press interactions on the remote are tracked. Only a UIKit predicate is needed for this. If you have a pure SwiftUI app but want to track remote presses on tvOS, you should also enable UIKit instrumentation.</li><li>The implementation differs between iOS 18+ and iOS 17 and below:<ul><li><strong>iOS 18 and above:</strong> Most interactions are reliably tracked with correct component names (for example, <code>SwiftUI_Button</code>, <code>SwiftUI_NavigationLink</code>).</li><li><strong>iOS 17 and below:</strong> The SDK cannot distinguish between interactive and non-interactive components (for example, Button vs. Label). For that reason, actions are reported as <code>SwiftUI_Unidentified_Element</code>.</li></ul></li><li>If you use both automatic and manual tracking, you may see duplicate events. This is a known limitation. To avoid this, use only one instrumentation type - either automatic or manual.</li><li>You can use the default predicate, <code>DefaultSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</code>, or provide your own to filter or rename actions. You can also disable legacy detection (iOS 17 and below) if you only want reliable iOS 18+ tracking:</li></ul><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Use the default predicate by disabling iOS 17 and below detection</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">predicate</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">DefaultSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">isLegacyDetectionEnabled</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Use your own predicate</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">CustomSwiftUIActionsPredicate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">SwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rumAction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">componentName</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">String</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMAction</span><span class="p">?</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="c1">// Custom logic to filter or rename actions</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMAction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">componentName</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Use the default predicate by disabling iOS 17 and below detection
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="n">DDDefaultSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="n">swiftUIActionsPredicate</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDDefaultSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">initWithIsLegacyDetectionEnabled</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">NO</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Use your own predicate
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="k">@protocol</span> <span class="nc">DDSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">NSObject</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="o">-</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DDRUMAction</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nullable</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="nl">rumActionFor</span><span class="p">:(</span><span class="n">NSString</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nonnull</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="n">componentName</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@interface</span> <span class="nc">CustomSwiftUIActionsPredicate</span> : <span class="nc">NSObject</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">DDSwiftUIRUMActionsPredicate</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@implementation</span> <span class="nc">CustomSwiftUIActionsPredicate</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">-</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DDRUMAction</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nullable</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="nf">rumActionFor:</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">NSString</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nonnull</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="nv">componentName</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="c1">// Custom logic to filter or rename actions
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMAction</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">initWithName</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">componentName</span> <span class="nl">attributes</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="l">@{}</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">@end</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><h4 id="action-reporting-by-ios-version">Action reporting by iOS version</h4><p>The table below shows how iOS 17 and iOS 18 report different user interactions.</p><table><thead><tr><th><strong>Component</strong></th><th><strong>iOS 18 reported name</strong></th><th><strong>iOS 17 reported name</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Button</td><td>SwiftUI_Button</td><td>SwiftUI_Unidentified_Element</td></tr><tr><td>NavigationLink</td><td>NavigationLink</td><td>SwiftUI_Unidentified_Element</td></tr><tr><td>Menu</td><td>SwiftUI_Menu (and its items as _UIContextMenuCell)</td><td>SwiftUI_Menu (and its items as _UIContextMenuCell)</td></tr><tr><td>Link</td><td>SwiftUI_Button</td><td>SwiftUI_Unidentified_Element</td></tr></tbody></table><h3 id="automatically-track-network-requests-2">Automatically track network requests</h3><p>Network requests are automatically tracked after you enable RUM with the <code>urlSessionTracking</code> configuration.</p><h4 id="optional-enable-detailed-timing-breakdown">(Optional) Enable detailed timing breakdown</h4><p>To get detailed timing breakdown (DNS resolution, SSL handshake, time to first byte, connection time, and download duration), enable <code>URLSessionInstrumentation</code> for your delegate type:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">URLSessionInstrumentation</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">enableDurationBreakdown</span><span class="p">(</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">delegateClass</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="p">&gt;.</span><span class="kc">self</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">session</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">URLSession</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">configuration</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="k">default</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">delegate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="p">&gt;(),</span>

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DDURLSessionInstrumentationConfiguration</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="n">config</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDURLSessionInstrumentationConfiguration</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">initWithDelegateClass</span><span class="p">:[</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="k">class</span><span class="p">]];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">DDURLSessionInstrumentation</span> <span class="nl">enableWithConfiguration</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">config</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                                      <span class="nl">delegate</span><span class="p">:[[</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="n">init</span><span class="p">]</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                                                 <span class="nl">delegateQueue</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">nil</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p><strong>Notes</strong>:</p><ul><li>Without <code>URLSessionInstrumentation</code>, network requests are still tracked. Enabling it provides detailed timing breakdown for performance analysis.</li><li>Response data is available in the <code>resourceAttributesProvider</code> callback (set in <code>RUM.Configuration.URLSessionTracking</code>) for tasks with completion handlers in automatic mode, and for all tasks after enabling <code>URLSessionInstrumentation</code>.</li><li>To filter out specific requests from being tracked, use the <code>resourceEventMapper</code> in <code>RUM.Configuration</code> (see <a href="#modify-or-drop-rum-events">Modify or drop RUM events</a>).</li></ul><div class="alert alert-info"><p>Be mindful of delegate retention. While Datadog instrumentation does not create memory leaks directly, it relies on <code>URLSession</code> delegates. According to <a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/foundation/urlsession/init(configuration:delegate:delegatequeue:)#parameters">Apple documentation</a>: &quot;The session object keeps a strong reference to the delegate until your app exits or explicitly invalidates the session. If you do not invalidate the session by calling the <code>invalidateAndCancel()</code> or <code>finishTasksAndInvalidate()</code> method, your app leaks memory until it exits.&quot; To avoid memory leaks, make sure to invalidate any <code>URLSession</code> instances you no longer need.</p></div><p>If you have more than one delegate type in your app that you want to instrument, you can call <code>URLSessionInstrumentation.enable(with:)</code> for each delegate type.</p><p>Also, you can configure first party hosts using <code>urlSessionTracking</code>. This classifies resources that match the given domain as &quot;first party&quot; in RUM and propagates tracing information to your backend (if you have enabled Tracing). Network traces are sampled with an adjustable sampling rate. A sampling of 20% is applied by default.</p><p>For instance, you can configure <code>example.com</code> as the first party host and enable both RUM and Tracing features:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">session</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">URLSession</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">configuration</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="k">default</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">delegate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="p">&gt;(),</span>

</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>This tracks all requests sent with the instrumented <code>session</code>. Requests matching the <code>example.com</code> domain are marked as &quot;first party&quot; and tracing information is sent to your backend to <a href="https://docs.datadoghq.com/real_user_monitoring/correlate_with_other_telemetry/apm?tab=browserrum">connect the RUM resource with its Trace</a>.</p></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">@</span><span class="n">import</span> <span class="n">DatadogRUM</span><span class="p">;</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DDRUMURLSessionTracking</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="n">urlSessionTracking</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="n">DDRUMURLSessionTracking</span> <span class="n">new</span><span class="p">];</span>

      </div><p>To add custom attributes to resources, use the <code>URLSessionTracking.resourceAttributesProvider</code> option when enabling the RUM. By setting attributes provider closure, you can return additional attributes to be attached to tracked resource.</p><p>For instance, you may want to add HTTP request and response headers to the RUM resource:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">enable</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">with</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Configuration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">...</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">urlSessionTracking</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Configuration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">URLSessionTracking</span><span class="p">(</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>If you don't want to track requests, you can disable URLSessionInstrumentation for the delegate type:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">URLSessionInstrumentation</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">disable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">delegateClass</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="p">&gt;.</span><span class="kc">self</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">DDURLSessionInstrumentation</span> <span class="nl">disableWithDelegateClass</span><span class="p">:[</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">YourSessionDelegate</span><span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="k">class</span><span class="p">]];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><h4 id="apollo-instrumentation-2">Apollo instrumentation</h4><p>Instrumenting Apollo in your iOS application gives RUM visibility into GraphQL errors and performance. Because GraphQL requests all go to a single endpoint and often return 200 OK even on errors, default HTTP instrumentation lacks context. It lets RUM capture the operation name, operation type, and variables (and optionally the payload). This provides more detailed context for each network request.</p><p>This integration supports both Apollo iOS 1.0+ and Apollo iOS 2.0+. Follow the instructions for the Apollo iOS version you have below.</p><ol><li><p><a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/ios">Set up</a> RUM monitoring with Datadog iOS RUM.</p></li><li><p>Add the following to your application's <code>Package.swift</code> file:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">dependencies</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="c1">// For Apollo iOS 1.0+</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">package</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios-apollo-interceptor&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">upToNextMajor</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">from</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;1.0.0&#34;</span><span class="p">))</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="c1">// For Apollo iOS 2.0+</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">package</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios-apollo-interceptor&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">upToNextMajor</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">from</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;2.0.0&#34;</span><span class="p">))</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">]</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Alternatively, you can add it using Xcode:</p><ol><li>Go to <strong>File</strong> → <strong>Add Package Dependencies</strong>.</li><li>Enter the repository URL: <code>https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-ios-apollo-interceptor</code>.</li><li>Select the package version that matches your Apollo major version (choose <code>1.x.x</code> for Apollo iOS 1.0+ or <code>2.x.x</code> for Apollo iOS 2.0+).</li></ol></li><li><p>Set up network instrumentation based on your Apollo iOS version:</p></li></ol><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="apollo-ios-10" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Apollo iOS 1.0+"><p>Set up network instrumentation for Apollo's built-in URLSessionClient:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">Apollo</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">graphQLInterceptors</span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">Operation</span><span class="p">&gt;(</span><span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">operation</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Operation</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="n">any</span> <span class="n">GraphQLInterceptor</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="k">where</span> <span class="n">Operation</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">GraphQLOperation</span> <span class="p">{</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>This lets Datadog RUM extract the operation type, name, variables, and payloads (optional) automatically from the requests to enrich GraphQL Requests RUM Resources.</p><div class="alert alert-info"><ul><li><p>The integration supports Apollo iOS versions <code>1.0+</code> and <code>2.0+</code>.</p></li><li><p>The <code>query</code> and <code>mutation</code> type operations are tracked; <code>subscription</code> operations are not.</p></li><li><p>GraphQL payload sending is disabled by default. To enable it, set the <code>sendGraphQLPayloads</code> flag in the <code>DatadogApolloInterceptor</code> constructor as follows:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">datadogInterceptor</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogApolloInterceptor</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sendGraphQLPayloads</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></li></ul></div><h3 id="automatically-track-errors">Automatically track errors</h3><p>All &quot;error&quot; and &quot;critical&quot; logs sent with <code>Logger</code> are automatically reported as RUM errors and linked to the current RUM view:</p><div class='code-tabs'>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="nl">setActionEventMapper</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">^</span><span class="n">DDRUMActionEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nullable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DDRUMActionEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nonnull</span> <span class="n">RUMActionEvent</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMActionEvent</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="nl">setLongTaskEventMapper</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">^</span><span class="n">DDRUMLongTaskEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nullable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DDRUMLongTaskEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nonnull</span> <span class="n">RUMLongTaskEvent</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMLongTaskEvent</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>Each mapper is a Swift closure with a signature of <code>(T) -&gt; T?</code>, where <code>T</code> is a concrete RUM event type. This allows changing portions of the event before it is sent.</p><p>For example, to redact sensitive information in a RUM Resource's <code>url</code>, implement a custom <code>redacted(_:) -&gt; String</code> function and use it in <code>resourceEventMapper</code>:</p><div class='code-tabs'>
      <ul class="nav nav-tabs d-flex"></ul>
        <div class="tab-content"><div data-lang="swift" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Swift"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">configuration</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">RUM</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Configuration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">applicationID</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;&lt;rum application id&gt;&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">resourceEventMapper</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span> <span class="k">in</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nv">RUMResourceEvent</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">resource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">url</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">redacted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">resource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div data-lang="objective-c" class="tab-pane fade" role="tabpanel" title="Objective-C"><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-objective-c"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DDRUMConfiguration</span> <span class="o">*</span><span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">DDRUMConfiguration</span> <span class="n">alloc</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="nl">initWithApplicationID</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s">@&#34;&lt;rum application id&gt;&#34;</span><span class="p">];</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="nl">setResourceEventMapper</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">^</span><span class="n">DDRUMResourceEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nullable</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DDRUMResourceEvent</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">_Nonnull</span> <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">RUMResourceEvent</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}];</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
      </div><p>Returning <code>nil</code> from the error, resource, or action mapper drops the event entirely; the event is not sent to Datadog. The value returned from the view event mapper must not be <code>nil</code> (to drop views, customize your implementation of <code>UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</code>; read more in <a href="#automatically-track-views">tracking views automatically</a>).</p><p>Depending on the event's type, only some specific properties can be modified:</p><table><thead><tr><th>Event Type</th><th>Attribute key</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>RUMActionEvent</td><td><code>RUMActionEvent.action.target?.name</code></td><td>Name of the action.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMActionEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this action.</td></tr><tr><td>RUMErrorEvent</td><td><code>RUMErrorEvent.error.message</code></td><td>Error message.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMErrorEvent.error.stack</code></td><td>Stacktrace of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMErrorEvent.error.resource?.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource the error refers to.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMErrorEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this error.</td></tr><tr><td>RUMResourceEvent</td><td><code>RUMResourceEvent.resource.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMResourceEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this resource.</td></tr><tr><td>RUMViewEvent</td><td><code>RUMViewEvent.view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMViewEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>RUMViewEvent.view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr></tbody></table><h2 id="retrieve-the-rum-session-id-2">Retrieve the RUM session ID</h2><p>Retrieving the RUM session ID can be helpful for troubleshooting.
