For example, you can attach the session ID to support requests, emails, or bug reports so that your support team can later find the user session in Datadog.</p><p>You can access the RUM session ID at runtime without waiting for the <code>sessionStarted</code> event:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">RumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">shared</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">currentSessionID</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">completion</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">sessionId</span> <span class="k">in</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">currentSessionId</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">sessionId</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">})</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="set-tracking-consent--gdpr-compliance">Set tracking consent (GDPR compliance)</h2><p>To be compliant with the GDPR regulation, the RUM iOS SDK requires the tracking consent value at initialization.</p><p>The <code>trackingConsent</code> setting can be one of the following values:</p><ol><li><code>.pending</code>: The RUM iOS SDK starts collecting and batching the data but does not send it to Datadog. The RUM iOS SDK waits for the new tracking consent value to decide what to do with the batched data.</li><li><code>.granted</code>: The RUM iOS SDK starts collecting the data and sends it to Datadog.</li><li><code>.notGranted</code>: The RUM iOS SDK does not collect any data. No logs, traces, or RUM events are sent to Datadog.</li></ol><p>To change the tracking consent value after the RUM iOS SDK is initialized, use the <code>Datadog.set(trackingConsent:)</code> API call. The RUM iOS SDK changes its behavior according to the new value.</p><p>For example, if the current tracking consent is <code>.pending</code>:</p><ul><li>If you change the value to <code>.granted</code>, the RUM iOS SDK sends all current and future data to Datadog;</li><li>If you change the value to <code>.notGranted</code>, the RUM iOS SDK wipes all current data and does not collect future data.</li></ul><h2 id="add-user-properties-2">Add user properties</h2><p>You can use the <code>Datadog.addUserExtraInfo(_:)</code> API to append extra user properties to previously set properties.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogCore</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addUserExtraInfo</span><span class="p">([</span><span class="s">&#34;company&#34;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">&#34;Foo&#34;</span><span class="p">])</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="data-management">Data management</h2><p>The iOS SDK first stores events locally and only uploads events when the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/ios/setup">intake specifications</a> conditions are met.</p><h3 id="clear-all-data-2">Clear all data</h3><p>You have the option of deleting all unsent data stored by the SDK with the <code>Datadog.clearAllData()</code> API.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogCore</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">clearAllData</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="stop-data-collection-2">Stop data collection</h3><p>You can use the <code>Datadog.stopInstance()</code> API to stop a named SDK instance (or the default instance if the name is <code>nil</code>) from collecting and uploading data further.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-swift"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">import</span> <span class="nc">DatadogCore</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">stopInstance</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Calling this method disables the SDK and all active features, such as RUM. To resume data collection, you must reinitialize the SDK. You can use this API if you want to change configurations dynamically.</p></div><div class="cdoc__toggleable cdoc__hidden" data-description="SDK is Flutter" data-if=cdocs-ref-3><p>If you have not set up the Datadog Flutter SDK for RUM yet, follow the <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">in-app setup instructions</a> or see the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/flutter/setup/">RUM Flutter setup documentation</a>. Learn how to set up <a href="#opentelemetry-setup">OpenTelemetry with RUM Flutter</a>. For additional manual instrumentation functions, such as automatic view tracking, see <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/flutter/integrated_libraries/">Flutter Libraries for RUM</a>.</p><h2 id="initialization-parameters-3">Initialization parameters</h2><p>You can specify the following parameters in your configuration when initializing the SDK.</p><dl><dt><code>clientToken</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>A client token for RUM or logging/APM. You can obtain this token in Datadog.</dd><dt><code>env</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The environment name sent to Datadog. You can use <code>env</code> to filter events by environment (for example, <code>staging</code> or <code>production</code>).</dd><dt><code>site</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br>The Datadog site that data is sent to. Enum values: <code>us1</code>, <code>us3</code>, <code>us5</code>, <code>eu1</code>, <code>us1Fed</code>, <code>ap1</code>, and <code>ap2</code>.</dd><dt><code>nativeCrashReportEnabled</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables native crash reporting.</dd><dt><code>service</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The service name for the application.</dd><dt><code>uploadFrequency</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>average</code><br>The frequency at which the Datadog SDK tries to upload data batches. Enum values: <code>frequent</code>, <code>average</code>, and <code>rare</code>.</dd><dt><code>batchSize</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>medium</code><br>Defines the Datadog SDK policy for batching data before uploading it to Datadog servers. Larger batches result in larger (but fewer) network requests. Smaller batches result in smaller (but more) network requests. Enum values: <code>small</code>, <code>medium</code>, and <code>large</code>.</dd><dt><code>batchProcessingLevel</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>medium</code><br>Defines the maximum number of batches processed sequentially without a delay, within one reading and uploading cycle. With higher levels, more data is sent in a single upload cycle, and more CPU and memory are used to process the data. With lower levels, less data is sent in a single upload cycle, and less CPU and memory are used to process the data. Enum values: <code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>, and <code>high</code>.</dd><dt><code>version</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The application's version number. Because <code>version</code> is a Datadog tag, it must comply with the rules in <a href="/getting_started/tagging/#defining-tags">Defining Tags</a>.</dd><dt><code>flavor</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The flavor (variant) of the application. For stack trace deobfuscation, this must match the flavor set during symbol upload.</dd><dt><code>firstPartyHosts</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: List&lt;String&gt;<br>A list of first party hosts, used in conjunction with Datadog network tracking packages. Overrides any values set in <code>firstPartyHostsWithTracinHeaders</code>. To specify different headers per host, use <code>firstPartyHostsWithTracingHeaders</code> instead.</dd><dt><code>firstPartyHostsWithTracingHeaders</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Map&lt;String, Set&lt;TracingHeaderType&gt;&gt;<br>A map of first party hosts and the types of tracing headers Datadog automatically injects on resource calls, used in conjunction with Datadog network tracking packages. For example:<div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="nl">clientToken:</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">CLIENT_TOKEN</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="nl">env:</span> <span class="err">`</span><span class="n">prod</span><span class="err">`</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="nl">site:</span> <span class="n">DatadogSite</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">us1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="nl">firstPartyHostsWithTracingHeaders:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="s1">&#39;example.com&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">TracingHeaderType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">b3</span><span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div>The <code>TracingHeaderType</code> enum has the following values:<ul><li><code>datadog</code>: Datadog's <a href="/real_user_monitoring/connect_rum_and_traces/?tab=browserrum#how-are-rum-resources-linked-to-traces"><code>x-datadog-*</code> header</a></li><li><code>b3</code>: OpenTelemetry B3 <a href="https://github.com/openzipkin/b3-propagation#single-headers">single header</a></li><li><code>b3multi</code>: OpenTelemetry B3 <a href="https://github.com/openzipkin/b3-propagation#multiple-headers">multiple headers</a></li><li><code>tracecontext</code>: W3C <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/trace-context/#tracestate-header">trace context header</a></li></ul></dd><dt><code>rumConfiguration</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Object<br>See <a href="#rum-configuration">RUM configuration</a>.</dd></dl><h3 id="rum-configuration-2">RUM configuration</h3><p>Use the following parameters for the <code>DatadogRumConfiguration</code> class.</p><dl><dt><code>applicationId</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The RUM application ID.</dd><dt><code>sessionSamplingRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Double<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>100.0</code><br>The sampling rate for RUM sessions. Must be between <code>0.0</code> (no RUM events are sent) and <code>100.0</code> (all RUM events are sent).</dd><dt><code>traceSampleRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Double<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>20.0</code><br>The sampling rate for resource tracing. Must be between <code>0.0</code> (no resources include APM tracing) and <code>100.0</code> (all resources include APM tracing).</dd><dt><code>traceContextInjection</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>all</code><br>The strategy for injecting trace context into requests. Enum values can be <code>all</code> (inject trace context into all requests) or <code>sampled</code> (inject trace context into only sampled requests).</dd><dt><code>detectLongTasks</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enable or disable long task detection. This capability attempts to detect when an application is doing too much work on the main isolate or native thread, which could prevent your app from rendering at a smooth framerate.</dd><dt><code>longTaskThreshold</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Double<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>0.1</code><br>The amount of elapsed time that distinguishes a <em>long task</em>, in seconds. If the main isolate takes more than this amount of time to process a microtask, it appears as a long task in Datadog RUM Explorer. Minimum value: <code>0.02</code>. On Flutter Web, which always uses a value of <code>0.05</code> seconds, this argument is ignored.</dd><dt><code>trackFrustrations</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enables <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/browser/frustration_signals/">automatic collection of user frustrations</a>.</dd><dt><code>vitalUpdateFrequency</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>average</code><br>The preferred frequency for collecting mobile vitals. Enum values: <code>frequent</code> (100ms),<code>average</code> (500ms), and <code>rare</code> (1000ms). To disable mobile vitals collection, set this parameter to <code>null</code>.</dd><dt><code>reportFlutterPerformance</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables reporting Flutter-specific performance metrics, including build and raster times.</dd><dt><code>customEndpoint</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>A custom endpoint for sending RUM data.</dd><dt><code>telemetrySampleRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Double<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>20.0</code><br>The sampling rate for telemetry data, such as errors and debug logs.</dd></dl><h2 id="tracking-from-background-isolates">Tracking from background isolates</h2><p>Starting with v3, Datadog Flutter SDK is capable of monitoring from multiple isolates, but monitoring must be initialized from the background isolate:</p><p>When initializing your background isolate, call <code>DatadogSdk.instance.attachToBackgroundIsolate</code>. For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Future</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="kt">void</span><span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="n">_spawnIsolate</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="kd">async</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">receivePort</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">ReceivePort</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">receivePort</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">listen</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="n">message</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">      <span class="c1">//
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="p">});</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kd">await</span> <span class="n">Isolate</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">spawn</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">_backgroundWork</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">receivePort</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">sendPort</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kt">void</span> <span class="n">_backgroundWork</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">SendPort</span> <span class="n">port</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kd">async</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="kd">await</span> <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">attachToBackgroundIsolate</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// Your background work
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><code>attachToBackgroundIsolate</code> must be called <strong>after</strong> Datadog is initialized in your main isolate, otherwise the call silently fails and tracking is not available.</p><p>If you are using <a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_tracking_http_client">Datadog Tracking HTTP Client</a> to automatically track resources, <code>attachToBackgroundIsolate</code> automatically starts tracking resources from the calling isolate. However, using <code>Client</code> from the <code>http</code> package or <code>Dio</code> requires you to re-initialize HTTP tracking for those packages from the background isolate.</p><h2 id="automatically-track-resources">Automatically track resources</h2><p>Use the <a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_tracking_http_client">Datadog Tracking HTTP Client</a> package to enable automatic tracking of resources and HTTP calls from your views.</p><p>Add the package to your <code>pubspec.yaml</code> and add the following to your initialization file:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// configuration
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>  <span class="nl">firstPartyHosts:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;example.com&#39;</span><span class="p">],</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)..</span><span class="n">enableHttpTracking</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><strong>Note</strong>: The Datadog Tracking HTTP Client modifies <a href="https://api.flutter.dev/flutter/dart-io/HttpOverrides/current.html"><code>HttpOverrides.global</code></a>. If you are using your own custom <code>HttpOverrides</code>, you may need to inherit from <a href="https://pub.dev/documentation/datadog_tracking_http_client/latest/datadog_tracking_http_client/DatadogTrackingHttpOverrides-class.html"><code>DatadogHttpOverrides</code></a>. In this case, you do not need to call <code>enableHttpTracking</code>. Versions of <code>datadog_tracking_http_client</code> &gt;= 1.3 check the value of <code>HttpOverrides.current</code> and use this for client creation, so you only need to make sure to initialize <code>HttpOverrides.global</code> prior to initializing Datadog.</p><p>To enable Datadog <a href="/serverless/aws_lambda/distributed_tracing/">distributed tracing</a>, you must set the <code>DatadogConfiguration.firstPartyHosts</code> property in your configuration object to a domain that supports distributed tracing. You can also modify the sampling rate for distributed tracing by setting the <code>traceSampleRate</code> on your <code>DatadogRumConfiguration</code>.</p><ul><li><p><code>firstPartyHosts</code> does not allow wildcards, but matches any subdomains for a given domain. For example, <code>api.example.com</code> matches <code>staging.api.example.com</code> and <code>prod.api.example.com</code>, not <code>news.example.com</code>.</p></li><li><p><code>DatadogRumConfiguration.traceSampleRate</code> sets a default sampling rate of 20%. If you want all resources requests to generate a full distributed trace, set this value to <code>100.0</code>.</p></li></ul><h3 id="track-resources-from-other-packages">Track resources from other packages</h3><p>While <code>Datadog Tracking HTTP Client</code> can track most common network calls in Flutter, Datadog supplies packages for integration into specific networking libraries, including gRPC, GraphQL and Dio. For more information about these libraries, see <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/flutter/integrated_libraries">Integrated Libraries</a>.</p><h2 id="enrich-user-sessions-3">Enrich user sessions</h2><p>Flutter RUM automatically tracks attributes such as user activity, views (using the <code>DatadogNavigationObserver</code>), errors, native crashes, and network requests (using the Datadog Tracking HTTP Client). See the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/flutter/data_collected">RUM Data Collection documentation</a> to learn about the RUM events and default attributes. You can further enrich user session information and gain finer control over the attributes collected by tracking custom events.</p><h3 id="notify-the-sdk-that-your-view-finished-loading">Notify the SDK that your view finished loading</h3><p>iOS RUM tracks the time it takes for your view to load. To notify the SDK that your view has finished loading, call the <code>addViewLoadingTime</code> method on <code>DatadogRum</code>. Call this method when your view is fully loaded and ready to be displayed to the user:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addViewLoadingTime</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">override</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Use the <code>override</code> option to replace the previously calculated loading time for the current view.</p><p>After the loading time is sent, it is accessible as <code>@view.loading_time</code> and is visible in the RUM UI.</p><p><strong>Note</strong>: This API is still experimental and might change in the future.</p><h3 id="add-your-own-performance-timing">Add your own performance timing</h3><p>In addition to RUM's default attributes, you can measure where your application is spending its time by using <code>DdRum.addTiming</code>. The timing measure is relative to the start of the current RUM view.</p><p>For example, you can time how long it takes for your hero image to appear:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kt">void</span> <span class="n">_onHeroImageLoaded</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addTiming</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;hero_image&#34;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>After you set the timing, it is accessible as <code>@view.custom_timings.&lt;timing_name&gt;</code>. For example, <code>@view.custom_timings.hero_image</code>.</p><p>To create visualizations in your dashboards, <a href="/real_user_monitoring/explorer/?tab=measures#setup-facets-and-measures">create a measure</a> first.</p><h3 id="track-user-actions">Track user actions</h3><p>You can track specific user actions such as taps, clicks, and scrolls using <code>DdRum.addAction</code>.</p><p>To manually register instantaneous RUM actions such as <code>RumActionType.tap</code>, use <code>DdRum.addAction()</code>. For continuous RUM actions such as <code>RumActionType.scroll</code>, use <code>DdRum.startAction()</code> or <code>DdRum.stopAction()</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kt">void</span> <span class="n">_downloadResourceTapped</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">String</span> <span class="n">resourceName</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addAction</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">RumActionType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">tap</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">resourceName</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>When using <code>DdRum.startAction</code> and <code>DdRum.stopAction</code>, the <code>type</code> action must be the same for the Datadog Flutter SDK to match an action's start with its completion.</p><h3 id="track-custom-resources">Track custom resources</h3><p>In addition to tracking resources automatically using the <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-flutter/tree/main/packages/datadog_tracking_http_client">Datadog Tracking HTTP Client</a>, you can track specific custom resources such as network requests or third-party provider APIs using the <a href="https://pub.dev/documentation/datadog_flutter_plugin/latest/datadog_flutter_plugin/">following methods</a>:</p><ul><li><code>DdRum.startResource</code></li><li><code>DdRum.stopResource</code></li><li><code>DdRum.stopResourceWithError</code></li><li><code>DdRum.stopResourceWithErrorInfo</code></li></ul><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in your network client:
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">startResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s2">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">RumHttpMethod</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="kd">get</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Later
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">stopResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s2">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="m">200</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">RumResourceType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">image</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>The <code>String</code> used for <code>resourceKey</code> in both calls must be unique for the resource you are calling in order for the Flutter Datadog SDK to match a resource's start with its completion.</p><h3 id="track-custom-errors">Track custom errors</h3><p>To track specific errors, notify <code>DdRum</code> when an error occurs with the message, source, exception, and additional attributes.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;This is an error message.&#34;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="track-custom-global-attributes-3">Track custom global attributes</h2><p>In addition to the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/flutter/data_collected">default RUM attributes</a> captured by the Datadog Flutter SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information (such as custom attributes) to your RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog.</p><p>Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (such as the cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, and network health).</p><h3 id="set-a-custom-global-attribute-2">Set a custom global attribute</h3><p>To set a custom global attribute, use <code>DdRum.addAttribute</code>.</p><ul><li>To add or update an attribute, use <code>DdRum.addAttribute</code>.</li><li>To remove the key, use <code>DdRum.removeAttribute</code>.</li></ul><h3 id="track-user-sessions-3">Track user sessions</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions makes it possible to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users</li></ul><a href="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?fit=max&amp;auto=format" class="pop" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#popupImageModal"><div class="shortcode-wrapper shortcode-img expand"><figure class="text-center"><picture style="width:90%"><img srcSet="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?auto=format" class="img-fluid" style="width:90%" alt="User API in the RUM UI"/></picture></figure></div></a><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use <code>DatadogSdk.setUserInfo</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setUserInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;1234&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">&#34;John Doe&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">&#34;john@doe.com&#34;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="add-custom-user-attributes">Add custom user attributes</h3><p>You can add custom attributes to your user session. This additional information is automatically applied to logs, traces, and RUM events.</p><p>To remove an existing attribute, set it to <code>null</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addUserExtraInfo</span><span class="p">({</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="s1">&#39;attribute_1&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;foo&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="s1">&#39;attribute_2&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="clear-all-data-3">Clear all data</h2><p>Use <code>clearAllData</code> to clear all data that has not been sent to Datadog.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">clearAllData</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="modify-or-drop-rum-events-3">Modify or drop RUM events</h2><p><strong>Note</strong>: This feature is not yet available for Flutter web applications.</p><p>To modify attributes of a RUM event before it is sent to Datadog or to drop an event entirely, use the Event Mappers API when configuring the Flutter RUM SDK:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">config</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="c1">// other configuration...
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nl">rumConfiguration:</span> <span class="n">DatadogRumConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nl">applicationId:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;YOUR_APPLICATION_ID&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">rumViewEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">rumActionEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">rumResourceEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">rumErrorEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">rumLongTaskEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">),</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Each mapper is a function with a signature of <code>(T) -&gt; T?</code>, where <code>T</code> is a concrete RUM event type. This allows changing portions of the event before it is sent, or dropping the event entirely.</p><p>For example, to redact sensitive information in a RUM Resource's <code>url</code>, implement a custom <code>redacted</code> function and use it in <code>rumResourceEventMapper</code>:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">rumResourceEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="n">resourceEvent</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">resourceEvent</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">resourceEvent</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">resource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">redacted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">resourceEvent</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">resource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">resourceEvent</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Returning <code>null</code> from the error, resource, or action mapper drops the event entirely; the event is not sent to Datadog. The value returned from the view event mapper must not be <code>null</code>.</p><p>Depending on the event's type, only some specific properties can be modified:</p><table><thead><tr><th>Event Type</th><th>Attribute key</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>RumViewEvent</td><td><code>viewEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>viewEvent.view.referrer</code></td><td>Referrer of the view.</td></tr><tr><td>RumActionEvent</td><td><code>actionEvent.action.target?.name</code></td><td>Name of the action.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>actionEvent.view.referrer</code></td><td>Referrer of the view linked to this action.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>actionEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this action.</td></tr><tr><td>RumErrorEvent</td><td><code>errorEvent.error.message</code></td><td>Error message.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.error.stack</code></td><td>Stacktrace of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.error.resource?.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource the error refers to.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.view.referrer</code></td><td>Referrer of the view linked to this action.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this error.</td></tr><tr><td>RumResourceEvent</td><td><code>resourceEvent.resource.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>resourceEvent.view.referrer</code></td><td>Referrer of the view linked to this action.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>resourceEvent.view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view linked to this resource.</td></tr></tbody></table><h2 id="retrieve-the-rum-session-id-3">Retrieve the RUM session ID</h2><p>Retrieving the RUM session ID can be helpful for troubleshooting. For example, you can attach the session ID to support requests, emails, or bug reports so that your support team can later find the user session in Datadog.</p><p>You can access the RUM session ID at runtime without waiting for the <code>sessionStarted</code> event:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">sessionId</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kd">await</span> <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rum</span><span class="o">?</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">getCurrentSessionId</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="flutter-specific-performance-metrics">Flutter-specific performance metrics</h2><p>To enable the collection of Flutter-specific performance metrics, set <code>reportFlutterPerformance: true</code> in <code>DatadogRumConfiguration</code>. Widget build and raster times are displayed in <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/mobile_vitals/?tab=flutter">Mobile Vitals</a>.</p><h2 id="opentelemetry-setup">OpenTelemetry setup</h2><p>All of Datadog's automatic network tracking packages (<a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_tracking_http_client">Datadog Tracking HTTP Client</a>, <a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_grpc_interceptor">gRPC Interceptor</a>, <a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_gql_link">GQL Link</a>, and <a href="https://pub.dev/packages/datadog_dio">Dio Interceptor</a>) support distributed traces through both automatic header generation and header ingestion. This section describes how to use OpenTelemetry with RUM Flutter.</p><h3 id="datadog-header-generation">Datadog header generation</h3><p>When configuring your tracking client or gRPC Interceptor, you can specify the types of tracing headers you want Datadog to generate. For example, if you want to send <code>b3</code> headers to <code>example.com</code> and <code>tracecontext</code> headers for <code>myapi.names</code>, you can do so with the following code:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">hostHeaders</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;example.com&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">TracingHeaderType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">b3</span> <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;myapi.names&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">TracingHeaderType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">tracecontext</span><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">};</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>You can use this object during initial configuration:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// For default Datadog HTTP tracing:
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="kd">final</span> <span class="n">configuration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="c1">// configuration
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nl">firstPartyHostsWithTracingHeaders:</span> <span class="n">hostHeaders</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>You can then enable tracing as usual.</p><p>This information is merged with any hosts set on <code>DatadogConfiguration.firstPartyHosts</code>. Hosts specified in <code>firstPartyHosts</code> generate Datadog Tracing Headers by default.</p><h2 id="check-first-party-hosts">Check first party hosts</h2><p>To determine if a specific URI is a first party host, use <code>isFirstPartyHost</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-dart"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kd">var</span> <span class="n">host</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">&#39;example.com&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">isFirstPartyHost</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">host</span><span class="p">)){</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="n">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;</span><span class="si">$</span><span class="n">host</span><span class="s1"> is a first party host.&#39;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="cdoc__toggleable cdoc__hidden" data-description="SDK is React Native" data-if=cdocs-ref-4><p>If you have not set up the SDK yet, follow the <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">in-app setup instructions</a> or see the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/react_native">React Native RUM setup documentation</a>.</p><h2 id="jest-testing">Jest testing</h2><p>Testing apps using <code>'@datadog/mobile-react-native'</code> might require completing extra steps, since Native Modules do not exist in testing environments.</p><p>Datadog provides mocks for the <code>'@datadog/mobile-react-native'</code> package. To use them with <a href="https://jestjs.io/">Jest</a>, add the following in your Jest setup file:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">jest</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">mock</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">require</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native/jest&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Interaction, error, and resource automated tracking is disabled in your tests if you initialize the SDK with the <code>DatadogProvider</code> component.</p><p>All SDK methods are mocked by <code>jest.fn()</code>, so you can assert that a Datadog SDK method was called:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">DdLogs</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">describe</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;App&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">it</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;calls DdLogs.debug on mount&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">renderer</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">create</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="nx">App</span> <span class="o">/&gt;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">expect</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">DdLogs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">debug</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="nx">toHaveBeenCalledWith</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;app started&#39;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">});</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>If you use a test runner other than Jest, you need to create the mocks for your test runner.</p><h2 id="initialization-parameters-4">Initialization parameters</h2><p>You can specify the following parameters in your configuration when initializing the SDK:</p><h3 id="core-configuration">Core configuration</h3><dl><dt><code>clientToken</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>A <a href="/account_management/api-app-keys/#client-tokens">Datadog client token</a>.</dd><dt><code>env</code></dt><dd>Required<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The application's environment, for example: prod, pre-prod, and staging. Follows the <a href="/getting_started/tagging/#define-tags">tag syntax requirements</a>.</dd><dt><code>rumConfiguration</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>RumConfiguration</code><br>The Datadog RUM configuration. RUM is <strong>disabled by default</strong>. See <a href="#rum-configuration">RUM configuration</a>.</dd><dt><code>logsConfiguration</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>LogsConfiguration</code><br>The Datadog Logs configuration. Logs is <strong>disabled by default</strong>: use an empty configuration <code>{}</code> to enable. See <a href="#logs-configuration">Logs configuration</a>.</dd><dt><code>traceConfiguration</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>TraceConfiguration</code><br>The Datadog Trace configuration. Trace is <strong>disabled by default</strong>: use an empty configuration <code>{}</code> to enable. See <a href="#trace-configuration">Trace configuration</a>.</dd><dt><code>site</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>US1</code><br><a href="/getting_started/site/">The Datadog site parameter of your organization</a>.</dd><dt><code>service</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The service name for your application. Follows the <a href="/getting_started/tagging/#define-tags">tag syntax requirements</a>.</dd><dt><code>verbosity</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: SdkVerbosity<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>Verbosity for internal SDK logging. Set to <code>SdkVerbosity.DEBUG</code> to debug your SDK implementation.</dd><dt><code>version</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The application's version. For example: 1.2.3, 6c44da20, and 2020.02.13. Follows the <a href="/getting_started/tagging/#define-tags">tag syntax requirements</a>.</dd><dt><code>versionSuffix</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>Add a suffix to the reported version of the app. Accepted characters are alphanumerics and <code>_</code>, <code>-</code>, <code>:</code>, <code>.</code>, <code>/</code>. Other special characters are converted to underscores. A dash (<code>-</code>) is automatically added between the version and the suffix. Follows the <a href="/getting_started/tagging/#define-tags">tag syntax requirements</a>.</dd><dt><code>proxyConfig</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: ProxyConfiguration<br>Optional <a href="/real_user_monitoring/guide/proxy-mobile-rum-data/">proxy configuration</a>.</dd><dt><code>uploadFrequency</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: UploadFrequency<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>UploadFrequency.AVERAGE</code><br>Sets the preferred frequency for uploading batches of data.</dd><dt><code>batchSize</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: BatchSize<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>BatchSize.MEDIUM</code><br>Defines the Datadog SDK policy when batching data together before uploading it to Datadog servers. Smaller batches mean smaller but more network requests, whereas larger batches mean fewer but larger network requests.</dd></dl><h3 id="rum-configuration-3">RUM configuration</h3><dl><dt><code>applicationId</code></dt><dd><strong>Required</strong><br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br>The RUM application ID.</dd><dt><code>trackInteractions</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables automatic collection of user actions.</dd><dt><code>trackResources</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables collection of resource events.</dd><dt><code>trackErrors</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables collection of React Native crashes.</dd><dt><code>trackFrustrations</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enables <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/browser/frustration_signals/">automatic collection of user frustrations</a>. Only error taps are supported. Implies <code>trackInteractions: true</code>.</dd><dt><code>sessionSampleRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>100</code><br>The percentage of sessions to track: <code>100</code> for all, <code>0</code> for none. Only tracked sessions send RUM events.</dd><dt><code>resourceTraceSampleRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>100</code><br>The percentage of requests to trace: <code>100</code> for all, <code>0</code> for none. For more information, see <a href="/real_user_monitoring/correlate_with_other_telemetry/apm?tab=reactnativerum">Connect RUM and Traces</a>.</dd><dt><code>nativeCrashReportEnabled</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables crash reporting for native platforms (iOS, Android).</dd><dt><code>nativeLongTaskThresholdMs</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number | false<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>200</code><br>The threshold for native long tasks reporting in milliseconds. Setting it to <code>0</code> or <code>false</code> disables native long task reporting. Values below <code>100</code> are raised to <code>100</code>. Values above <code>5000</code> are lowered to <code>5000</code>.</dd><dt><code>nativeViewTracking</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables native views tracking. Set to <code>true</code> if you use a custom navigation system relying on native views.</dd><dt><code>nativeInteractionTracking</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables native interaction tracking. Set to <code>true</code> if you want to track interactions on native screens.</dd><dt><code>firstPartyHosts</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: List<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>[]</code><br>List of your backends hosts to enable tracing with. For more information, see <a href="/real_user_monitoring/correlate_with_other_telemetry/apm?tab=reactnativerum">Connect RUM and Traces</a>.</dd><dt><code>telemetrySampleRate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>20</code><br>Telemetry data (such as errors and debug logs) about SDK execution is sent to Datadog to detect and solve potential issues. Set this option to <code>0</code> to opt out from telemetry collection.</dd><dt><code>longTaskThresholdMs</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number | false<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>0</code><br>The threshold for JavaScript long tasks reporting in milliseconds. Setting it to <code>0</code> or <code>false</code> disables JavaScript long task reporting. Values below <code>100</code> are raised to <code>100</code>. Values above <code>5000</code> are lowered to <code>5000</code>.</dd><dt><code>vitalsUpdateFrequency</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: VitalsUpdateFrequency<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>VitalsUpdateFrequency.AVERAGE</code><br>Sets the preferred frequency for collecting mobile vitals.</dd><dt><code>trackBackgroundEvents</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Enables tracking of RUM event when no RUM View is active. By default, background events are not tracked. Enabling this feature might increase the number of sessions tracked and impact your billing.</dd><dt><code>useAccessibilityLabel</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Determines whether the accessibility labels are used to name RUM actions (default is true).</dd><dt><code>trackNonFatalAnrs</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code> on Android 29 and below, <code>false</code> on Android 30+.<br>Enables tracking of non-fatal ANRs on Android. By default, the reporting of non-fatal ANRs on Android 30+ is disabled because it would create too much noise over fatal ANRs. On Android 29 and below, however, the reporting of non-fatal ANRs is enabled by default, as fatal ANRs cannot be reported on those versions.</dd><dt><code>trackWatchdogTerminations</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>false</code><br>Determines whether the SDK should track application termination by the watchdog on iOS.</dd><dt><code>trackMemoryWarnings</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enables tracking of memory warnings as RUM events on iOS. When enabled, the SDK automatically records a RUM event each time the app receives a memory warning from the operating system.</dd><dt><code>appHangThreshold</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>The app hang threshold in seconds for non-fatal app hangs on iOS. App hangs are an iOS-specific type of error that happens when the application is unresponsive for too long. By default, app hangs reporting is disabled, but you can enable it and set your own threshold to monitor app hangs that last more than a specified duration by using this parameter. Set the <code>appHangThreshold</code> parameter to the minimal duration you want app hangs to be reported. For example, enter 0.25 to report hangs lasting at least 250 ms. See <a href="/real_user_monitoring/error_tracking/mobile/ios/?tab=cocoapods#configure-the-app-hang-threshold">Configure the app hang threshold</a> for more guidance on what to set this value to.</dd><dt><code>initialResourceThreshold</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Number<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>0.1</code> (seconds)<br>The amount of time after a view starts where a Resource should be considered when calculating Time to Network-Settled (TNS). TNS is calculated using all resources that start within the specified threshold, in seconds.</dd><dt><code>errorEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>ErrorEventMapper</code><br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>null</code><br>Custom function to modify the attributes of a RUM Error event before it is sent to Datadog.</dd><dt><code>actionEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>ActionEventMapper</code><br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>null</code><br>Custom function to modify the attributes of a RUM Action event before it is sent to Datadog.</dd><dt><code>resourceEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>ResourceEventMapper</code><br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>null</code><br>Custom function to modify the attributes of a RUM Resource event before it is sent to Datadog.</dd><dt><code>customEndpoint</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>Sets a target custom server for RUM.</dd></dl><h3 id="logs-configuration">Logs configuration</h3><dl><dt><code>bundleLogsWithRum</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enables RUM correlation with logs (default is true).</dd><dt><code>bundleLogsWithTraces</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Boolean<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>true</code><br>Enables trace correlation with logs.</dd><dt><code>logEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: <code>LogEventMapper</code><br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>null</code><br>Custom function to modify the attributes of a Log event before it is sent to Datadog.</dd><dt><code>customEndpoint</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>Sets a target custom server for Logs.</dd></dl><h3 id="trace-configuration">Trace configuration</h3><dl><dt><code>customEndpoint</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>Sets a target custom server for Traces.</dd></dl><h2 id="manual-instrumentation">Manual instrumentation</h2><p>If automatic instrumentation doesn't suit your needs, you can manually create RUM Events and Logs:</p><h3 id="send-logs">Send logs</h3><p>When you instrument your code to send logs, it can include debug, info, warn, or error details:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdLogs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">debug</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet…&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{});</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdLogs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">info</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet…&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{});</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdLogs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">warn</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet…&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{});</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdLogs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">error</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet…&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="manually-track-rum-views">Manually track RUM views</h3><p>To manually track RUM Views, provide a <code>view key</code>, <code>view name</code>, and <code>action name</code> at initialization. Depending on your needs, you can choose one of the following strategies:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">startView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;view-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;View Name&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">//…
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">stopView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;view-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">custom</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">42</span> <span class="p">},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="manually-track-rum-actions">Manually track RUM actions</h3><p>You can manually track RUM actions:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addAction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">RumActionType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">TAP</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;action name&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>To track a continuous action:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">startAction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">RumActionType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">TAP</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;action name&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">//...
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">stopAction</span><span class="p">({},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="manually-track-rum-errors">Manually track RUM errors</h3><p>You can manually track RUM errors:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;message&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">ErrorSource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">SOURCE</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;stacktrace&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="manually-track-rum-resources">Manually track RUM resources</h3><p>You can manually track RUM resources:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">startResource</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;res-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;GET&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;http://www.example.com/api/v1/test&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">//...
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">stopResource</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;res-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">200</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;xhr&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">size</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1337</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="p">{},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="notify-the-sdk-that-your-view-finished-loading-2">Notify the SDK that your view finished loading</h3><p>You can notify the SDK that your view has finished loading by calling the <code>addViewLoadingTime</code> method on <code>DdRum</code>. Call this method when your view is fully loaded and ready to be displayed to the user:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addViewLoadingTime</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Use the <code>overwrite</code> parameter to replace the previously calculated loading time for the current view.</p><p>After the loading time is sent, it is accessible as <code>@view.loading_time</code> and is visible in the RUM UI.</p><p><strong>Note</strong>: This API is experimental.</p><h3 id="add-custom-timings">Add custom timings</h3><p>You can add custom timings:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addTiming</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;timing-name&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="manually-send-spans">Manually send spans</h3><p>You can send spans manually:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">spanId</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kr">await</span> <span class="nx">DdTrace</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">startSpan</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;foo&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">custom</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">42</span> <span class="p">},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">//...
