</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdTrace</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">finishSpan</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">spanId</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">custom</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">21</span> <span class="p">},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="track-custom-global-attributes-4">Track custom global attributes</h2><p>You can attach user information to all RUM events to get more detailed information from your RUM sessions.</p><h3 id="track-user-sessions-4">Track user sessions</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions makes it possible to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users</li></ul><a href="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?fit=max&amp;auto=format" class="pop" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#popupImageModal"><div class="shortcode-wrapper shortcode-img expand"><figure class="text-center"><picture><img srcSet="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?auto=format" class="img-fluid" alt="User API in RUM UI"/></picture></figure></div></a><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.extraInfo</code></td><td>Object</td><td>(Optional) Include custom attributes such as subscription type, any user specific information that enhance user context in RUM sessions.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use the <code>setUserInfo</code> API, for example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">setUserInfo</span><span class="p">({</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">id</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;1337&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">name</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;John Smith&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">email</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;john@example.com&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">extraInfo</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">type</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;premium&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>If you want to add or update user information, you can use the following code to modify the existing user's details.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addUserExtraInfo</span><span class="p">({</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">hasPaid</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;true&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>If you want to clear the user information (for example, when the user signs out), you can do so by calling the <code>clearUserInfo</code> API:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">clearUserInfo</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="global-attributes">Global attributes</h3><p>You can keep global attributes to track information about a specific session, such as A/B testing configuration, ad campaign origin, or cart status. These attributes are attached to all future Logs, Spans, and RUM events.</p><p><strong>Add multiple global attributes</strong></p><p>Use <code>addAttributes</code> to add or update several attributes at once.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addAttributes</span><span class="p">({</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">profile_mode</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;wall&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">chat_enabled</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">campaign_origin</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;example_ad_network&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><strong>Add a single global attribute</strong></p><p>Use <code>addAttribute</code> when you want to add or update a single attribute.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addAttribute</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;profile_mode&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;wall&#39;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">addAttribute</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;chat_enabled&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>If the attribute already exists, its value is overwritten.</p><p><strong>Remove a single global attribute</strong></p><p>Use <code>removeAttribute</code> to remove a specific attribute from the global context.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">removeAttribute</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;campaign_origin&#39;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>After removal, the attribute is no longer attached to future Logs, Spans, or RUM events.</p><p><strong>Remove multiple global attributes</strong></p><p>Use <code>removeAttributes</code> to remove several attributes at once.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">removeAttributes</span><span class="p">([</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;profile_mode&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;chat_enabled&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">]);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>This is useful when cleaning up session-specific data, such as when a user logs out or exits a feature flow.</p><h2 id="track-view-navigation">Track view navigation</h2><p>Because React Native offers a wide range of libraries to create screen navigation, only manual view tracking is supported by default. To see RUM or Error tracking sessions populate in Datadog, you need to implement view tracking.</p><p>You can manually start and stop a view using the following <code>startView()</code> and <code>stopView</code> methods.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DdRum</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Start a view with a unique view identifier, a custom view name, and an object to attach additional attributes to the view
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">startView</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;view-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// &lt;view-key&gt; has to be unique, for example it can be ViewName-unique-id
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="s1">&#39;View Name&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">{</span> <span class="s1">&#39;custom.foo&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;something&#39;</span> <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Stops a previously started view with the same unique view identifier, and an object to attach additional attributes to the view
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">stopView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">&#39;&lt;view-key&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="s1">&#39;custom.bar&#39;</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">42</span> <span class="p">},</span> <span class="nb">Date</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">now</span><span class="p">());</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Use one of Datadog's integrations to automatically track views for the following libraries:</p><ul><li>If you use the <a href="https://github.com/wix/react-native-navigation"><code>react-native-navigation</code></a> library, then add the <code>@datadog/mobile-react-native-navigation</code> package and follow the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/react_native/integrated_libraries/">setup instructions</a>.</li><li>If you use the <a href="https://github.com/react-navigation/react-navigation"><code>react-navigation</code></a> library, then add the <code>@datadog/mobile-react-navigation</code> package and follow the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/react_native/integrated_libraries/">setup instructions</a>.</li></ul><p>If you experience any issues setting up View tracking with <code>@datadog/mobile-react-navigation</code> you can see this Datadog <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-reactnative-examples/tree/main/rum-react-navigation">example application</a> as a reference.</p><h2 id="clear-all-data-4">Clear all data</h2><p>Use <code>clearAllData</code> to clear all data that has not been sent to Datadog.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">DdSdkReactNative</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">clearAllData</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="modify-or-drop-rum-events-4">Modify or drop RUM events</h2><p>To modify attributes of a RUM event before it is sent to Datadog, or to drop an event entirely, use the Event Mappers API when configuring the RUM React Native SDK:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">SdkVerbosity</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProviderConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">LogsConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">TraceConfiguration</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">config</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="nx">DatadogProviderConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;CLIENT_TOKEN&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;ENVIRONMENT_NAME&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">rumConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="nx">applicationId</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;APPLICATION_ID&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="nx">trackInteractions</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Track user interactions (such as a tap on buttons).
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>            <span class="nx">trackResources</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Track XHR resources
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>            <span class="nx">trackErrors</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Track errors
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>            <span class="c1">// RUM Event Mappers
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>            <span class="nx">errorEventMapper</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="nx">resourceEventMapper</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="nx">actionEventMapper</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="nx">event</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="c1">// Log Event Mappers
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>        <span class="nx">logsConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="nx">logEventMapper</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="nx">event</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">traceConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Each mapper is a function with a signature of <code>(T) -&gt; T?</code>, where <code>T</code> is a concrete RUM event type. This allows changing portions of the event before it is sent, or dropping the event entirely.</p><p>For example, to redact sensitive information from a RUM error <code>message</code>, implement a custom <code>redacted</code> function and use it in <code>errorEventMapper</code>:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nx">config</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">rumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">errorEventMapper</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">message</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">redacted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">message</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">};</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Returning <code>null</code> from the error, resource, or action mapper drops the event entirely; the event is not sent to Datadog.</p><p>Depending on the event type, only some specific properties can be modified:</p><table><thead><tr><th>Event Type</th><th>Attribute key</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>LogEvent</td><td><code>logEvent.message</code></td><td>Message of the log.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>logEvent.context</code></td><td>Custom attributes of the log.</td></tr><tr><td>ActionEvent</td><td><code>actionEvent.context</code></td><td>Custom attributes of the action.</td></tr><tr><td>ErrorEvent</td><td><code>errorEvent.message</code></td><td>Error message.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.source</code></td><td>Source of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.stacktrace</code></td><td>Stacktrace of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.context</code></td><td>Custom attributes of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.timestampMs</code></td><td>Timestamp of the error.</td></tr><tr><td>ResourceEvent</td><td><code>resourceEvent.context</code></td><td>Custom attributes of the resource.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>Events include additional context:</p><table><thead><tr><th>Event Type</th><th>Context attribute key</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>LogEvent</td><td><code>logEvent.additionalInformation.userInfo</code></td><td>Contains the global user info set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.setUserInfo</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>logEvent.additionalInformation.attributes</code></td><td>Contains the global attributes set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.addAttributes</code>.</td></tr><tr><td>ActionEvent</td><td><code>actionEvent.actionContext</code></td><td><a href="https://github.com/DefinitelyTyped/DefinitelyTyped/blob/683ec4a2b420ff6bd3873a7338416ad3ec0b6595/types/react-native-side-menu/index.d.ts#L2">GestureResponderEvent</a> corresponding to the action or <code>undefined</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>actionEvent.additionalInformation.userInfo</code></td><td>Contains the global user info set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.setUserInfo</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>actionEvent.additionalInformation.attributes</code></td><td>Contains the global attributes set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.addAttributes</code>.</td></tr><tr><td>ErrorEvent</td><td><code>errorEvent.additionalInformation.userInfo</code></td><td>Contains the global user info set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.setUserInfo</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>errorEvent.additionalInformation.attributes</code></td><td>Contains the global attributes set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.addAttributes</code>.</td></tr><tr><td>ResourceEvent</td><td><code>resourceEvent.resourceContext</code></td><td><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/XMLHttpRequest">XMLHttpRequest</a> corresponding to the resource or <code>undefined</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>resourceEvent.additionalInformation.userInfo</code></td><td>Contains the global user info set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.setUserInfo</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>resourceEvent.additionalInformation.attributes</code></td><td>Contains the global attributes set by <code>DdSdkReactNative.addAttributes</code>.</td></tr></tbody></table><h2 id="retrieve-the-rum-session-id-4">Retrieve the RUM session ID</h2><p>Retrieving the RUM session ID can be helpful for troubleshooting. For example, you can attach the session ID to support requests, emails, or bug reports so that your support team can later find the user session in Datadog.</p><p>You can access the RUM session ID at runtime with:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-javascript"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">DdRum</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">rumSessionId</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kr">await</span> <span class="nx">DdRum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">getCurrentSessionId</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="resource-timings">Resource timings</h2><p>Resource tracking provides the following timings:</p><ul><li><code>First Byte</code>: The time between the scheduled request and the first byte of the response. This includes time for the request preparation on the native level, network latency, and the time it took the server to prepare the response.</li><li><code>Download</code>: The time it took to receive a response.</li></ul><h2 id="initializing-asynchronously">Initializing asynchronously</h2><p>If your app includes a lot of animations when it starts, running code during these animations might delay them on some devices. To delay the Datadog React Native SDK for RUM to run after all current animations are started, set the <code>initializationMode</code> to <code>InitializationMode.ASYNC</code> in your configuration:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProviderConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">InitializationMode</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">RumConfiguration</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">datadogConfiguration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="nx">DatadogProviderConfiguration</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;CLIENT_TOKEN&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;ENVIRONMENT_NAME&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">initializationMode</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="nx">InitializationMode</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">ASYNC</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">rumConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">applicationId</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;APPLICATION_ID&gt;&#39;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">export</span> <span class="k">default</span> <span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">App</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span> <span class="nx">configuration</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nx">datadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="nx">Navigation</span> <span class="o">/&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="err">/DatadogProvider&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>This uses React Native's <a href="https://reactnative.dev/docs/interactionmanager#runafterinteractions">InteractionManager.runAfterInteractions</a> to delay the animations.</p><p>All interactions with the RUM SDK (view tracking, actions, resources tracing, and so on) are still recorded and kept in a queue with a limit of 100 events.</p><p>Logs are not recorded and calling a <code>DdLogs</code> method before the actual initialization might break logging.</p><p>If you experience any issue setting up the asynchronous initialization of Datadog, see the <a href="https://github.com/DataDog/dd-sdk-reactnative-examples/tree/main/rum-react-navigation-async">example application</a>.</p><h2 id="delaying-the-initialization">Delaying the initialization</h2><p>There may be situations where you want to wait before initializing the SDK. For example, when you want to use a different configuration based on the user role or to fetch the configuration from one of your servers.</p><p>In that case, you can auto-instrument your app from the start (automatically collect user interactions, XHR resources, and errors) and record up to 100 RUM and span events before initializing the SDK.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">DatadogProviderConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">PropagatorType</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">datadogAutoInstrumentation</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">rumConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">resourceTraceSampleRate</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">100</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">trackErrors</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">trackInteractions</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">trackResources</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">firstPartyHosts</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">[</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                <span class="nx">match</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;example.com&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                <span class="nx">propagatorTypes</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">[</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    <span class="nx">PropagatorType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">DATADOG</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    <span class="nx">PropagatorType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">TRACECONTEXT</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                <span class="p">]</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">],</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">};</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">initializeApp</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kr">async</span> <span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="kr">const</span> <span class="nx">configuration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kr">await</span> <span class="nx">fetchDatadogConfiguration</span><span class="p">();</span> <span class="c1">// Fetches the configuration from one of your servers
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="kr">await</span> <span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">initialize</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">configuration</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">};</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">export</span> <span class="k">default</span> <span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">App</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nx">useEffect</span><span class="p">(()</span> <span class="p">=&gt;</span> <span class="nx">initializeApp</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="p">[]);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="nx">DatadogProvider</span> <span class="nx">configuration</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nx">datadogAutoInstrumentation</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="nx">Navigation</span> <span class="o">/&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="err">/DatadogProvider&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>Where your configuration has the following keys:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-js"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kr">import</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="nx">ProxyConfiguration</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">SdkVerbosity</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">TrackingConsent</span> <span class="p">}</span> <span class="nx">from</span> <span class="s1">&#39;@datadog/mobile-react-native&#39;</span><span class="p">;</span>

Default = undefined
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nx">trackingConsent</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="nx">TrackingConsent</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">GRANTED</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: disable collection if user has not granted consent for tracking. Default = TrackingConsent.GRANTED
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nx">verbosity</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="nx">SdkVerbosity</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">WARN</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: let the SDK print internal logs (above or equal to the provided level). Default = undefined (no logs)
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nx">proxyConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="nx">ProxyConfiguration</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: send requests through a proxy. Default = undefined,
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nx">site</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;US1&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: specify Datadog site. Default = &#39;US1&#39;
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="nx">rumConfiguration</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">applicationId</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="s1">&#39;&lt;RUM_APPLICATION_ID&gt;&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nx">sessionSampleRate</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">80</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: sample RUM sessions (here, 80% of session will be sent to Datadog). Default = 100%
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>        <span class="nx">nativeViewTracking</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// Optional: enables tracking of native views. Default = false

</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">};</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="hybrid-app-monitoring">Hybrid app monitoring</h2><p>See <a href="/real_user_monitoring/guide/monitor-hybrid-react-native-applications">Monitor hybrid React Native applications</a>.</p></div><div class="cdoc__toggleable cdoc__hidden" data-description="SDK is Kotlin Multiplatform" data-if=cdocs-ref-5><p>If you have not set up the SDK yet, follow the <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">in-app setup instructions</a> or see the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform">Kotlin Multiplatform RUM setup documentation</a>.</p><h2 id="enrich-user-sessions-4">Enrich user sessions</h2><p>Kotlin Multiplatform RUM automatically tracks attributes such as user activity, screens, errors, and network requests. See the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/data_collected">RUM Data Collection documentation</a> to learn about the RUM events and default attributes. You can further enrich user session information and gain finer control over the attributes collected by tracking custom events.</p><h3 id="custom-views-3">Custom views</h3><p>In addition to <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/advanced_configuration/#automatically-track-views">tracking views automatically</a>, you can also track specific distinct views (such as activities and fragments) manually. Stop tracking when the view is no longer visible.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// to start view
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">startView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">viewKey</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">viewName</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">viewAttributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// to stop view
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">stopView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">viewKey</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">viewAttributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="add-your-own-performance-timing-2">Add your own performance timing</h3><p>In addition to RUM's default attributes, you can measure where your application is spending its time by using the <code>addTiming</code> API. The timing measure is relative to the start of the current RUM view. For example, you can time how long it takes for your hero image to appear:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">onHeroImageLoaded</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">addTiming</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;hero_image&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>After the timing is sent, the timing is accessible as <code>@view.custom_timings.&lt;timing_name&gt;</code>. For example: <code>@view.custom_timings.hero_image</code>. You must <a href="/real_user_monitoring/explorer/search/#setup-facets-and-measures">create a measure</a> before graphing it in RUM analytics or in dashboards.</p><h3 id="custom-actions-3">Custom actions</h3><p>In addition to <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/advanced_configuration/#initialization-parameters">tracking actions automatically</a>, you can also track specific custom user actions (such as taps, clicks, and scrolls) with <code>RumMonitor#addAction</code>. For continuous action tracking (for example, tracking a user scrolling a list), use <code>RumMonitor#startAction</code> and <code>RumMonitor#stopAction</code>.</p><p>The action type should be one of the following: &quot;custom&quot;, &quot;click&quot;, &quot;tap&quot;, &quot;scroll&quot;, &quot;swipe&quot;, &quot;back&quot;.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">onUserInteraction</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">addAction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">actionType</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">name</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">actionAttributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="enrich-resources-2">Enrich resources</h3><p>When <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/#initialize-rum-ktor-plugin-to-track-network-events-made-with-ktor">tracking resources automatically</a>, provide a custom <code>RumResourceAttributesProvider</code> instance to add custom attributes to each tracked network request/response. For example, if you want to track a network request's headers, create an implementation like the following, and pass it in the <code>datadogKtorPlugin</code> initialization call.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">class</span> <span class="nc">CustomRumResourceAttributesProvider</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">RumResourceAttributesProvider</span> <span class="p">{</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">names</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">associateWith</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="k">it</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">}.</span><span class="n">mapKeys</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="s2">&#34;header.</span><span class="si">$it</span><span class="s2">&#34;</span> <span class="p">}</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">override</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">onError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">request</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">HttpRequestSnapshot</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">throwable</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Throwable</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">emptyMap</span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">String</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Any</span><span class="p">?&gt;()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>

</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">datadogKtorPlugin</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="n">tracedHosts</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">mapOf</span><span class="p">(</span>
