</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="p">),</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="n">rumResourceAttributesProvider</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">CustomRumResourceAttributesProvider</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="custom-resources-3">Custom resources</h3><p>In addition to <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/#initialize-rum-ktor-plugin-to-track-network-events-made-with-ktor">tracking resources automatically</a>, you can also track specific custom resources (such as network requests and third-party provider APIs) with methods (such as <code>GET</code> and <code>POST</code>) while loading the resource with <code>RumMonitor#startResource</code>. Stop tracking with <code>RumMonitor#stopResource</code> when it is fully loaded, or <code>RumMonitor#stopResourceWithError</code> if an error occurs while loading the resource.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">loadResource</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">startResource</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">resourceKey</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">method</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">resourceAttributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">try</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="c1">// do load the resource
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>        <span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">stopResource</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">resourceKey</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">resourceKind</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">additionalAttributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">catch</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Exception</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">stopResourceWithError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">resourceKey</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">message</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">origin</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><strong>Note</strong>: <code>stopResource</code> / <code>stopResourceWithError</code> methods accepting <code>NSURLConnection</code> and <code>NSError</code> are also available from iOS source set.</p><h3 id="custom-errors-3">Custom errors</h3><p>To track specific errors, notify the monitor when an error occurs with the message, source, exception, and additional attributes. See the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/data_collected">Attributes collected documentation</a>.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">addError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">message</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">source</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">throwable</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">attributes</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><strong>Note</strong>: <code>addError</code> method accepting <code>NSError</code> is also available from iOS source set.</p><h3 id="add-user-properties-3">Add user properties</h3><p>You can use the <code>addUserExtraInfo</code> API to append extra user properties to previously set properties.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">addUserExtraInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">extraInfo</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="event-and-data-management-2">Event and data management</h2><p>The Kotlin Multiplatform SDK first stores events. It only uploads these events when the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/#sending-data-when-device-is-offline">intake specification</a> conditions are met.</p><h3 id="clear-all-data-5">Clear all data</h3><p>You have the option of deleting all unsent data stored by the SDK with the <code>clearAllData</code> API.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">clearAllData</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="stop-data-collection-3">Stop data collection</h3><p>You can use the <code>stopInstance</code> API to stop the SDK instance from collecting and uploading data further.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">stopInstance</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="set-remote-log-threshold-2">Set remote log threshold</h3><p>You can define the minimum log level (priority) to send events to Datadog in a logger instance. If the log priority is below the one you set at this threshold, it does not get sent. The default value is to allow all.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">logger</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nc">Logger</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setRemoteLogThreshold</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nc">LogLevel</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">INFO</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">build</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="track-custom-global-attributes-5">Track custom global attributes</h2><p>In addition to the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/kotlin_multiplatform/data_collected">default RUM attributes</a> captured by the RUM Kotlin Multiplatform SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information, such as custom attributes, to your RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog. Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (such as cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, and network health).</p><h3 id="track-user-sessions-5">Track user sessions</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions helps you to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users</li></ul><a href="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?fit=max&amp;auto=format" class="pop" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#popupImageModal"><div class="shortcode-wrapper shortcode-img expand"><figure class="text-center"><picture><img srcSet="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?auto=format" class="img-fluid" alt="User API in RUM UI"/></picture></figure></div></a><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use the <code>setUserInfo</code> API, for example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">Datadog</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setUserInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="m">1234</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">John</span> <span class="n">Doe</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="n">john</span><span class="nd">@doe</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">com</span><span class="err">&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="track-attributes-2">Track attributes</h3><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Adds an attribute to all future RUM events
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">addAttribute</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">key</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="k">value</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Removes an attribute to all future RUM events
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">removeAttribute</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">key</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="track-background-events-2">Track background events</h2><p>You can track events such as crashes and network requests when your application is in the background (for example, no active view is available).</p><p>Add the following snippet during RUM configuration:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">trackBackgroundEvents</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">true</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><div class="alert alert-info"><p>Tracking background events may lead to additional sessions, which can impact billing. For questions, <a href="https://docs.datadoghq.com/help/">contact Datadog support</a>.</p></div><h2 id="initialization-parameters-5">Initialization parameters</h2><p>You can use the following methods in <code>Configuration.Builder</code> when creating the Datadog configuration to initialize the library:</p><dl><dt><code>useSite(DatadogSite)</code></dt><dd>Switches target data to EU, US1, US3, US5, US1_FED, AP1, and AP2 sites.</dd><dt><code>setBatchSize([SMALL|MEDIUM|LARGE])</code></dt><dd>Defines the individual batch size for requests sent to Datadog.</dd><dt><code>setUploadFrequency([FREQUENT|AVERAGE|RARE])</code></dt><dd>Defines the frequency for requests made to Datadog endpoints (if requests are available).</dd><dt><code>setBatchProcessingLevel(LOW|MEDIUM|HIGH)</code></dt><dd>Defines the number of batches sent in each upload cycle.</dd><dt><code>trackCrashes(Boolean)</code></dt><dd>Allows you to control whether JVM/iOS crashes are tracked or not. The default value is <code>true</code>.</dd></dl><p>You can use the following methods in <code>RumConfiguration.Builder</code> when creating the RUM configuration to enable RUM features:</p><h3 id="common-configuration-methods">Common configuration methods</h3><dl><dt><code>trackLongTasks(durationThreshold)</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking tasks taking longer than <code>durationThreshold</code> on the main thread as long tasks in Datadog. See <a href="#automatically-track-long-tasks">Automatically track long tasks</a> for more information.</dd><dt><code>setVitalsUpdateFrequency([FREQUENT|AVERAGE|RARE|NEVER])</code></dt><dd>Sets the preferred frequency for collecting mobile vitals.</dd><dt><code>setSessionSampleRate(&lt;sampleRate&gt;)</code></dt><dd>Sets the RUM sessions sample rate. (A value of 0 means no RUM events are sent. A value of 100 means all sessions are kept.)</dd><dt><code>setSessionListener(RumSessionListener)</code></dt><dd>Sets a listener to be notified on when a new RUM Session starts.</dd><dt><code>setTelemetrySampleRate</code></dt><dd>The sampling rate for the SDK internal telemetry utilized by Datadog. This must be a value between <code>0</code> and <code>100</code>. By default, this is set to <code>20</code>.</dd><dt><code>setViewEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the ViewEventMapper for the RUM ViewEvent. You can use this interface implementation to modify the ViewEvent attributes before serialization.</dd><dt><code>setResourceEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the EventMapper for the RUM ResourceEvent. You can use this interface implementation to modify the ResourceEvent attributes before serialization.</dd><dt><code>setActionEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the EventMapper for the RUM ActionEvent. You can use this interface implementation to modify the ActionEvent attributes before serialization.</dd><dt><code>setErrorEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the EventMapper for the RUM ErrorEvent. You can use this interface implementation to modify the ErrorEvent attributes before serialization.</dd><dt><code>setLongTaskEventMapper</code></dt><dd>Sets the EventMapper for the RUM LongTaskEvent. You can use this interface implementation to modify the LongTaskEvent attributes before serialization.</dd><dt><code>trackBackgroundEvents</code></dt><dd>Enable/disable tracking RUM events when no activity is happening in the foreground. By default, background events are not tracked. Enabling this feature might increase the number of sessions tracked, and therefore your billing.</dd><dt><code>trackFrustrations</code></dt><dd>Enable/disable tracking of frustration signals.</dd></dl><h3 id="android-configuration-methods">Android configuration methods</h3><p>These methods can be accessed only from Android source set.</p><dl><dt><code>trackNonFatalAnrs(Boolean)</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking non-fatal ANRs. This is enabled by default on Android API 29 and below, and disabled by default on Android API 30 and above.</dd><dt><code>trackUserInteractions(Array&lt;ViewAttributesProvider&gt;)</code></dt><dd>Enables tracking user interactions (such as tap, scroll, or swipe). The parameter also allows you to add custom attributes to the RUM Action events based on the widget with which the user interacted.</dd><dt><code>useViewTrackingStrategy(strategy)</code></dt><dd>Defines the strategy used to track views. See <a href="#automatically-track-views">Automatically track views</a> for more information.</dd></dl><h3 id="ios-configuration-methods">iOS configuration methods</h3><dl><dt><code>trackUiKitViews(UIKitRUMViewsPredicate)</code></dt><dd>Enable automatic tracking of <code>UIViewController</code>s as RUM views. See <a href="#automatically-track-views">Automatically track views</a> for more information.</dd><dt><code>trackUiKitActions(UIKitRUMActionsPredicate)</code></dt><dd>Enable automatic tracking of <code>UITouch</code> events as RUM actions. The predicate implementation should return RUM action parameters if the given interaction should be accepted, or <code>null</code> to ignore it. By default, all touches are accepted.</dd><dt><code>setAppHangThreshold(Long)</code></dt><dd>Enables app hangs monitoring with the given threshold (in milliseconds). See <a href="/real_user_monitoring/error_tracking/mobile/ios/#add-app-hang-reporting">Add app hang reporting</a> for more information.</dd></dl><h3 id="automatically-track-views-3">Automatically track views</h3><h4 id="android">Android</h4><p>To automatically track your views (such as activities and fragments), provide a tracking strategy at initialization. Depending on your application's architecture, you can choose one of the following strategies:</p><dl><dt><code>ActivityViewTrackingStrategy</code></dt><dd>Every activity in your application is considered a distinct view.</dd><dt><code>FragmentViewTrackingStrategy</code></dt><dd>Every fragment in your application is considered a distinct view.</dd><dt><code>MixedViewTrackingStrategy</code></dt><dd>Every activity or fragment in your application is considered a distinct view.</dd><dt><code>NavigationViewTrackingStrategy</code></dt><dd>Recommended for Android Jetpack Navigation library users. Each Navigation destination is considered a distinct view.</dd></dl><p>For instance, to set each fragment as a distinct view, use the following configuration in your <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">setup</a>:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in common source set
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">rumConfig</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">applicationId</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">apply</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">platformSpecificSetup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">this</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">build</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">internal</span> <span class="k">expect</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">platformSpecificSetup</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">rumConfigurationBuilder</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in Android source set
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span><span class="k">internal</span> <span class="k">actual</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">platformSpecificSetup</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">rumConfigurationBuilder</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">rumConfigurationBuilder</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">useViewTrackingStrategy</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">FragmentViewTrackingStrategy</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="p">.)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>For <code>ActivityViewTrackingStrategy</code>, <code>FragmentViewTrackingStrategy</code>, or <code>MixedViewTrackingStrategy</code>, you can filter which <code>Fragment</code> or <code>Activity</code> is tracked as a RUM View by providing a <code>ComponentPredicate</code> implementation in the constructor:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">strategy</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">ActivityViewTrackingStrategy</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">trackExtras</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="k">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">componentPredicate</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="k">object</span> <span class="err">: </span><span class="nc">ComponentPredicate</span><span class="p">&lt;</span><span class="n">Activity</span><span class="p">&gt;</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">override</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">accept</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">component</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Activity</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="n">Boolean</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">true</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">override</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">getViewName</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">component</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Activity</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="n">String</span><span class="p">?</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="k">null</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p><strong>Note</strong>: By default, the library is using <code>ActivityViewTrackingStrategy</code>. If you decide not to provide a view tracking strategy, you must manually send the views by calling the <code>startView</code> and <code>stopView</code> methods yourself.</p><h4 id="ios">iOS</h4><p>To automatically track views (<code>UIViewController</code>s), use the <code>trackUiKitViews</code> method when enabling RUM. By default, views are named with the view controller's class name. To customize it, provide your own implementation of the <code>uiKitViewsPredicate</code> that conforms to <code>UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</code> interface.</p><p>Inside the <code>createView(viewController: UIViewController)</code> implementation, your app should decide if a given <code>UIViewController</code> instance should start the RUM view (return value) or not (return <code>null</code>). The returned <code>RUMView</code> value must specify the <code>name</code> and may provide additional <code>attributes</code> for the created RUM view.</p><p>For instance, you can configure the predicate to use explicit type check for each view controller in your app:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">class</span> <span class="nc">YourCustomPredicate</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIKitRUMViewsPredicate</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="k">override</span> <span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">createView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">viewController</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">UIViewController</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">?</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="k">when</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">viewController</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">          <span class="k">is</span> <span class="n">HomeViewController</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;Home&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">          <span class="k">is</span> <span class="n">DetailsViewController</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">RUMView</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&#34;Details&#34;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">          <span class="k">else</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="k">null</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>You can even come up with a more dynamic solution depending on your app's architecture.</p><p><strong>Note</strong>: By default, UIKit view tracking is not enabled.</p><h3 id="automatically-track-long-tasks-2">Automatically track long tasks</h3><p>Long running operations performed on the main thread can impact the visual performance and reactivity of your application. To track these operations, define the duration threshold above which a task is considered too long.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">rumConfig</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">applicationId</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// …
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">trackLongTasks</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">durationThreshold</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">build</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>For example, to replace the default <code>100 ms</code> duration, set a custom threshold in your configuration.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">rumConfig</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">applicationId</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// …
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">trackLongTasks</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="m">250L</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">// track tasks longer than 250ms as long tasks
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">build</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="modify-or-drop-rum-events-5">Modify or drop RUM events</h2><p>To modify some attributes in your RUM events, or to drop some of the events entirely before batching, provide an implementation of <code>EventMapper&lt;T&gt;</code> when initializing the RUM Kotlin Multiplatform SDK:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">rumConfig</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nc">RumConfiguration</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Builder</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">applicationId</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// ...
</span></span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1"></span>  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setErrorEventMapper</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rumErrorEventMapper</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setActionEventMapper</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rumActionEventMapper</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setResourceEventMapper</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rumResourceEventMapper</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setViewEventMapper</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rumViewEventMapper</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">setLongTaskEventMapper</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rumLongTaskEventMapper</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="p">.</span><span class="n">build</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>When implementing the <code>EventMapper&lt;T&gt;</code> interface, only some attributes are modifiable for each event type:</p><table><thead><tr><th>Event type</th><th>Attribute key</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>ViewEvent</td><td><code>view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr><tr><td>ActionEvent</td><td><code>action.target.name</code></td><td>Target name.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr><tr><td>ErrorEvent</td><td><code>error.message</code></td><td>Error message.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>error.stack</code></td><td>Stacktrace of the error.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>error.resource.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr><tr><td>ResourceEvent</td><td><code>resource.url</code></td><td>URL of the resource.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr><tr><td>LongTaskEvent</td><td><code>view.referrer</code></td><td>URL that linked to the initial view of the page.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.url</code></td><td>URL of the view.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td><code>view.name</code></td><td>Name of the view.</td></tr></tbody></table><p><strong>Note</strong>: If you return null from the <code>EventMapper&lt;T&gt;</code> implementation, the event is dropped.</p><h2 id="retrieve-the-rum-session-id-5">Retrieve the RUM session ID</h2><p>Retrieving the RUM session ID can be helpful for troubleshooting. For example, you can attach the session ID to support requests, emails, or bug reports so that your support team can later find the user session in Datadog.</p><p>You can access the RUM session ID at runtime without waiting for the <code>sessionStarted</code> event:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-kotlin"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="nc">GlobalRumMonitor</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="k">get</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">getCurrentSessionId</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">sessionId</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">currentSessionId</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">sessionId</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="cdoc__toggleable cdoc__hidden" data-description="SDK is Roku" data-if=cdocs-ref-6><p>If you have not set up the SDK yet, follow the <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">in-app setup instructions</a> or see the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/roku/setup">Roku RUM setup documentation</a>.</p><h2 id="track-rum-resources">Track RUM resources</h2><h3 id="rourltransfer">roUrlTransfer</h3><p>Network requests made directly with a <code>roUrlTransfer</code> node must be tracked.</p><p>For <em>synchronous requests</em>, you can use Datadog's <code>datadogroku_DdUrlTransfer</code> wrapper to track the resource automatically. This wrapper supports most features of the <code>roUrlTransfer</code> component, but does not support anything related to async network calls.</p><p>For example, here's how to do a <code>GetToString</code> call:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-text"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">    ddUrlTransfer = datadogroku_DdUrlTransfer(m.global.datadogRumAgent)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    ddUrlTransfer.SetUrl(url)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    ddUrlTransfer.EnablePeerVerification(false)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    ddUrlTransfer.EnableHostVerification(false)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    result = ddUrlTransfer.GetToString()
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>For <em>asynchronous requests</em>, automatic instrumentation is not supported. You need to track the resource manually. The following code snippet shows how to report the request as a RUM Resource:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-text"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">sub performRequest()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    m.port = CreateObject(&#34;roMessagePort&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    request = CreateObject(&#34;roUrlTransfer&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    &#39; setup the node url, headers, …
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    timer = CreateObject(&#34;roTimespan&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    timer.Mark()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    request.AsyncGetToString()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    while (true)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        msg = wait(1000, m.port)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        if (msg &lt;&gt; invalid)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            msgType = type(msg)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            if (msgType = &#34;roUrlEvent&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                if (msg.GetInt() = 1) &#39; transfer complete
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    durationMs&amp; = timer.TotalMilliseconds()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    transferTime# = datadogroku_millisToSec(durationMs&amp;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    httpCode = msg.GetResponseCode()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    status = &#34;ok&#34;
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    if (httpCode &lt; 0)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        status = msg.GetFailureReason()
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    end if
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    resource = {
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        url: requestUrl
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        method: &#34;GET&#34;
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        transferTime: transferTime#
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        httpCode: httpCode
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                        status: status
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    }
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                    m.global.datadogRumAgent.callfunc(&#34;addResource&#34;, resource)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">                end if
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            end if
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        end if
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    end while
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">end sub
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="streaming-resources">Streaming resources</h3><p>Whenever you use a <code>Video</code> or an <code>Audio</code> node to stream media, you can forward all <code>roSystemLogEvent</code> you receive to Datadog as follows:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-text"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">    sysLog = CreateObject(&#34;roSystemLog&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    sysLog.setMessagePort(m.port)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    sysLog.enableType(&#34;http.error&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    sysLog.enableType(&#34;http.complete&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    while(true)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        msg = wait(0, m.port)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        if (type(msg) = &#34;roSystemLogEvent&#34;)
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">            m.global.datadogRumAgent.callfunc(&#34;addResource&#34;, msg.getInfo())
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        end if
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    end while
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="enrich-user-sessions-5">Enrich user sessions</h2><p>After your Roku channel is instrumented with RUM, you can further enrich user session information and gain finer control over the attributes collected by tracking custom events.</p><p>In addition to the default RUM attributes captured by the RUM Roku SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information, such as custom attributes, to your RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog. Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (such as cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, or network health).</p><h3 id="identifying-your-users">Identifying your users</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions makes it possible to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user.</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors.</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users.</li></ul><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use the <code>datadogUserInfo</code> global field, after initializing the SDK, for example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-text"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">    m.global.setField(&#34;datadogUserInfo&#34;, { id: 42, name: &#34;Abcd Efg&#34;, email: &#34;abcd.efg@example.com&#34;})
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="track-custom-global-attributes-6">Track custom global attributes</h3><p>In addition to the default attributes captured by the SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information, such as custom attributes, to your Logs and RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog. Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (for example by cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, and network health).</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-text"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl">    m.global.setField(&#34;datadogContext&#34;, { foo: &#34;Some value&#34;, bar: 123})
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="cdoc__toggleable cdoc__hidden" data-description="SDK is Unity" data-if=cdocs-ref-7><p>If you have not set up the Datadog Unity SDK for RUM yet, follow the <a href="https://app.datadoghq.com/rum/application/create">in-app setup instructions</a> or see the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/unity/setup/">RUM Unity setup documentation</a>. Learn how to set up <a href="#opentelemetry-setup">OpenTelemetry with RUM Unity</a>.</p><h3 id="advanced-initialization-options">Advanced initialization options</h3><dl><dt><code>Custom Endpoint</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: String<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>undefined</code><br>Send data to a custom endpoint instead of the default Datadog endpoint. This is useful for proxying data through a custom server.</dd><dt><code>SDK Verbosity</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Enum<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>Warn</code><br>The level of debugging information the Datadog SDK should output. Higher levels output more information. This option is helpful for getting debugging information from the SDK when something is not working as expected, or removing the SDK-related debugging entries from console logs.</dd><dt><code>Telemetry Sample Rate</code></dt><dd>Optional<br><strong>Type</strong>: Double<br><strong>Default</strong>: <code>20</code><br>The percentage rate at which Datadog sends internal telemetry data. A value of 100 means all telemetry data is sampled and sent to Datadog.</dd></dl><h3 id="automatic-view-tracking">Automatic view tracking</h3><p>If you select <code>Enable Automatic Scene Tracking</code>, Datadog hooks into Unity's <code>SceneManager</code> to detect scenes loading and unloading, and start RUM Views appropriately. If you are using methods to move between scenes other than <code>SceneManager</code>, or would like to track changes in views that occur without <code>SceneManager</code>, you need to track views manually using <code>DdRum.StartView</code> and <code>DdRum.StopView</code>.</p><h3 id="track-user-actions-2">Track user actions</h3><p>You can track specific user actions such as taps, clicks, and scrolls using <code>DdRum.AddAction</code>.</p><p>To manually register instantaneous RUM actions such as <code>RumActionType.Tap</code>, use <code>DdRum.AddAction()</code>. For continuous RUM actions such as <code>RumActionType.Scroll</code>, use <code>DdRum.StartAction()</code> or <code>DdRum.StopAction()</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">void</span> <span class="n">DownloadResourceTapped</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">string</span> <span class="n">resourceName</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">AddAction</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">RumActionType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Tap</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">        <span class="n">resourceName</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>When using <code>DdRum.StartAction</code> and <code>DdRum.StopAction</code>, the <code>type</code> action must be the same for the Datadog Unity SDK to match an action's start with its completion.</p><h3 id="track-resources">Track resources</h3><p>Datadog provides <code>DatadogTrackedWebRequest</code> as a drop in replacement for <code>UnityWebRequest</code> to enable tracking of resources and HTTP calls from your RUM views.</p><p>You can use it the same way as you would any other <code>UnityWebRequest</code>:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="kt">var</span> <span class="n">request</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">DatadogTrackedWebRequest</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#34;https://httpbin.org/headers&#34;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">yield</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">SendWebRequest</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">Debug</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Log</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#34;Got result: &#34;</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">downloadHandler</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">text</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="track-custom-resources-2">Track custom resources</h3><p>In addition to tracking resources automatically using <code>DatadogTrackedWebRequest</code>, you can track specific custom resources such as network requests or third-party provider APIs using the following methods:</p><ul><li><code>DdRum.StartResource</code></li><li><code>DdRum.StopResource</code></li><li><code>DdRum.StopResourceWithError</code></li><li><code>DdRum.StopResourceWithErrorInfo</code></li></ul><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// in your network client:</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">StartResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">RumHttpMethod</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Get</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="c1">// Later</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">StopResource</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="s">&#34;resource-key&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="m">200</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">    <span class="n">RumResourceType</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Image</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><p>The <code>string</code> used for <code>resourceKey</code> in both calls must be unique for the resource you are calling in order for the Unity Datadog SDK to match a resource's start with its completion.</p><h3 id="track-custom-errors-2">Track custom errors</h3><p>To track specific errors, notify <code>DdRum</code> when an error occurs with the exception, the source, and any additional attributes.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">try</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="c1">// Error prone code</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="k">catch</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Exception</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl">  <span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Rum</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">AddError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">RumErrorSource</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Source</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">}</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="track-custom-global-attributes-7">Track custom global attributes</h2><p>In addition to the <a href="/real_user_monitoring/application_monitoring/unity/data_collected/">default RUM attributes</a> captured by the Datadog Unity SDK automatically, you can choose to add additional contextual information (such as custom attributes) to your RUM events to enrich your observability within Datadog.</p><p>Custom attributes allow you to filter and group information about observed user behavior (such as the cart value, merchant tier, or ad campaign) with code-level information (such as backend services, session timeline, error logs, and network health).</p><h3 id="set-a-custom-global-attribute-3">Set a custom global attribute</h3><p>To set a custom global attribute, use <code>DdRum.AddAttribute</code>.</p><ul><li>To add or update an attribute, use <code>DdRum.AddAttribute</code>.</li><li>To remove the key, use <code>DdRum.RemoveAttribute</code>.</li></ul><h3 id="track-user-sessions-6">Track user sessions</h3><p>Adding user information to your RUM sessions makes it possible to:</p><ul><li>Follow the journey of a given user</li><li>Know which users are the most impacted by errors</li><li>Monitor performance for your most important users</li></ul><a href="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?fit=max&amp;auto=format" class="pop" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#popupImageModal"><div class="shortcode-wrapper shortcode-img expand"><figure class="text-center"><picture style="width:90%"><img srcSet="http://localhost:1313/images/real_user_monitoring/browser/advanced_configuration/user-api.73b0cac9af174bfd4322133367d6e968.png?auto=format" class="img-fluid" style="width:90%" alt="User API in the RUM UI"/></picture></figure></div></a><table><thead><tr><th>Attribute</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>usr.id</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Required) Unique user identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.name</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User friendly name, displayed by default in the RUM UI.</td></tr><tr><td><code>usr.email</code></td><td>String</td><td>(Optional) User email, displayed in the RUM UI if the user name is not present.</td></tr></tbody></table><p>To identify user sessions, use <code>DatadogSdk.SetUserInfo</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">SetUserInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#34;1234&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&#34;John Doe&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&#34;john@doe.com&#34;</span><span class="p">);</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h3 id="add-custom-user-attributes-2">Add custom user attributes</h3><p>You can add custom attributes to your user session. This additional information is automatically applied to logs, traces, and RUM events.</p><p>To remove an existing attribute, set it to <code>null</code>.</p><p>For example:</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">AddUserExtraInfo</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">new</span> <span class="p">()</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">{</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="s">&#34;attribute_1&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&#34;foo&#34;</span> <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="s">&#34;attribute_2&#34;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="k">null</span> <span class="p">},</span>
</span></span><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="p">});</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><h2 id="clear-all-data-6">Clear all data</h2><p>Use <code>ClearAllData</code> to clear all data that has not been sent to Datadog.</p><div class="code-snippet-wrapper"><div class="code-filename-wrapper d-flex justify-content-end"></div><div class="code-snippet "><div class="code-button-wrapper position-absolute"><button class="btn text-primary js-copy-button">Copy</button></div><div class="cdoc-code-snippet cdoc-language-csharp"><pre tabindex="0" class="chroma"><code><span class="line"><span class="cl"><span class="n">DatadogSdk</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">instance</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">ClearAllData</span><span class="p">();</span>
</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></article></div>
